Commentary

A Study of Korean Migration to the Northeast

(Continuation 9) Bin

(2) Unlimited Expansion of Japanese Police Power: Wherever Koreans set foot in our Northeast, Japanese police power expands along with them. Japanese often instigate unscrupulous elements among Korean residents to engage in various illegal activities that endanger our country. We have no way to stop them. For example, in mid-April of this year, Wu Renhua, a translator at the Anti-Communist Affairs Office of the Northeast Border Defense Army's Deputy Commander's Office in Jilin, was shot and killed by a Japanese Korean, Jin Zhengyuan. Afterwards, Jin Zhengyuan took refuge in the Japanese consulate. After repeated negotiations, there were no results. The case remains unresolved. For example, American journalist Mr. Colorwell investigated that under the protection and connivance of the Japanese police, Japanese and Korean residents in Harbin actually used the Japanese post office in the Manchurian Railway Zone to send opium, morphine, heroin and other drugs. Dedicated persons were also sent to sell them along the China Eastern Railway. In Anda alone, there were more than 60 semi-public places set up by Japanese and Koreans to sell drugs. If our authorities arrest them, the Japanese police will intervene, and the Japanese consul will protest, so there is no way to prohibit them. Eventually, drugs spread everywhere. All these illegal acts and improper businesses of the Koreans occur under the connivance of the Japanese police and the protection of Japanese legal authority. There are accumulated cases that cannot be resolved.

(3) Nationality Disputes of Korean Residents: The Tanaka Memorial, quoted earlier, states: "... The naturalized Koreans, although nominally naturalized citizens of China, will soon return to our nationality... This is only because of temporary convenience that they become citizens of China.... In addition, among the Koreans in Manchuria and Mongolia, some have naturalized as citizens of China, while others have not. When the time comes, whether it is Korean citizens of Chinese nationality who cause trouble or Korean citizens of Japanese nationality who cause trouble, we can use the strategy of 'selling dog meat under the banner of sheep's head' to deal with it..." These words are no less than a confession of the Japanese conspiracy to use Koreans with dual nationality to disturb us. Today, as soon as Koreans enter our country, they form villages. Within a village, naturalized and non-naturalized residents live together. The good people can still cultivate the land to support themselves. Those who are cunning and sly will act recklessly and do anything. They live on our land and eat our food. But if we exercise our ruling power, they will instigate the non-naturalized residents to resist. If we treat them as outside the law, they will claim Chinese nationality and openly rent and buy land. Even worse, most Koreans have already naturalized in our country and are also registered as Japanese nationals at the same time. One person has dual nationality. These Koreans are sometimes Chinese and sometimes Japanese, changing constantly, all following the instructions of the Japanese. When land disputes and civil and criminal lawsuits occur between Koreans and Chinese in the Northeast, Koreans often rely on their dual nationality status to seek the protection of the Japanese. They are instigated by the Japanese to undermine our country's judiciary. Conversely, if Koreans commit crimes in Korea, they often use the Eastern Provinces as a place of refuge. Japanese soldiers often clash with our people when arresting Koreans, causing our people to suffer various unexpected damages. Koreans seek convenience by holding dual nationality, and the Japanese take advantage of this to create excuses to plot attacks. This is insidious and malicious, and it is especially harmful to the Northeast.

(4) Koreans Disturbing Local Security: Most of the Koreans who have migrated to our Northeast are poor. Many of them are able to work hard in agriculture, but there are also many who willingly become bandits and rely on the protection of Japanese police power to undermine the security of our Northeast. Their firearms have a Japanese source, and their concealment is protected by the Japanese. It is difficult for our local authorities to investigate and govern them.

There is nothing we can do about them. Koreans get the name, we get the harm, and the Japanese applaud from the side, deeply rejoicing in the success of their plan.

In summary, the harm that Korean migration causes to our Northeast can already be seen. The future is long, and the troubles will be endless. Therefore, can our country not quickly devise countermeasures for remedy? (To be continued)

News

Sixth Plenary Session of the National Government

▲ Promulgation of the Banknote Issuance Tax Law

▲ Appointment of Liao Weifan as Director of the Capital Rehabilitation Institute

The National Government held its sixth plenary session on the morning of the 31st day of the month. The members present were Yu Youren, Zhu Peide, Cai Yuanpei, Wang Boqun, Wang Zhengting, Ding Weifen, Ma Fuxiang, and Shao Yuanchong. Yu Youren chaired the meeting. The matters discussed were: (1) Resolved that Article 13 of the Factory Law will be allowed a two-year preparation period for implementation, and the Ministry of Industry will be responsible for supervision and urging; (2) Resolved to promulgate the Banknote Issuance Tax Law; (3) Resolved to promulgate the Bank Earnings Tax Law; (4) Resolved to appoint Liao Weifan as Director of the Capital Rehabilitation Institute; (5) The Ministry of Finance reported that the depreciation of banknotes in Shanxi Province has a significant impact on the province's finances. It has been repeatedly approved for the provincial government to reinstate the issuance of the Shanxi Gold Industry Public Bonds that had been abolished, so it should be approved for reinstatement to provide relief. The revised regulations of the public bonds have been prepared and submitted for review and implementation. It was resolved to submit it to the Legislative Yuan.

Further News on the Communist Suppression Army Recapturing Donggu

▲ Besieged and Attacked by Over 200,000 Troops

▲ Cai Tingkai Led His Troops to Enter Donggu First

▲ The Communist Nest Was Completely Destroyed by the Various Armies

▲ The Remaining Communist Troops Fled Towards Ruijin and Yudu

Nanchang Dispatch: The situation of the recapture of Donggu has been reported in yesterday's news. Now, more detailed information has been obtained, which is recorded as follows:

Looking back at the Communist Suppression Army's plan, the goal was to eliminate the main force of the Red Bandits. Therefore, the right wing and the central route advanced to the communist nests in Donggu, Wangpi, Luokou, Xiaopu, Longgang, and Shaxi. The progress was initially very slow, while the officers and soldiers of the left wing, which encircled the Red Bandits on the border of Jiangxi and Fujian, advanced lightly and quickly, traveling over a hundred li or seventy or eighty li per day. After taking Ningdu and entering Xingguo to the southeast of Donggu, they cut off the Red Bandits' retreat to the south. The right wing and the central route then rushed towards the communist nests. Therefore, within a few days, they suddenly recaptured the deeply rooted old nest of the Red Bandits in Donggu. After the Communist Suppression Army captured Shicheng and Ningdu, the Red Bandits, except for the two units of Zhu De and Xiang Ying, who fled into Tingzhou and Ninghua in Fujian, Peng Dehuai and Mao Zedong, entrenched themselves in Ruijin, Yudu, and Dongshanba. In the battles of Wenhui, Xianrenqiao, and Shicheng, the Peng Mao bandits retreated to Shaxi, Longgang, Dongshao, Luokou, and Wangpi, and joined forces with the pseudo-army of Gu Daozhong and Li Wenlin, who were guarding the old nest, in an attempt to make a final stand. At that time, Commander-in-Chief Chiang ordered He Yingqin and Chen Mingshu to lead the group armies of the left and right wings to encircle and suppress them on a large scale. He and Chen made separate arrangements. The first route army of the left wing, Zhao Guantao's troops, advanced from Ningdu to Gulonggang in Xingguo, and then advanced north from Qingtangkantian, the intersection of Ningdu, Yudu, and Xingguo, directly attacking the old nest of the Red Bandits in Wangpi and Xiaopu, north of Ningdu, taking the form of a pincer attack with Sun Lianzhong's troops from the central route from Le'an to Ningdu. The second route army advanced from Ningdu and Yudu to Jiangkou, cutting off the path for the Red Bandits to flee to Ruijin. Then, they went west from Liangcun and Yuexi in Yongfeng to attack Longgang. At the same time, Zhu Shaoliang of the Third Army sent a part of his troops to launch a fierce attack on Luokou via Toupi, the northwestern border of Guangchang. Gao Shuxun's troops took Wangpi and Xiaopu. The Second and Tenth Armies of the Fourth Army Corps were deployed in Shicheng, Ningdu, Ruijin, and the Fujian border to block the bandits in Donggu from fleeing south into Fujian and to prevent side attacks from the bandits in Ninghua, Tingzhou, and Ruijin. The right-wing army, with the Jiang and Cai divisions of the 19th Route Army as the main force attacking Donggu, went straight from Futian to Donggu. Sun Lianzhong's 25th and 27th Divisions attacked from Yihuang and Le'an to the north of Ningdu and the east of Yongfeng to surround the east of Donggu. The Hao Mengling and Han Deqin units of the Third Route Army took Baishui, Shuikou, Tengtian, Baisha, Shaxi, and Shima from Jishui and Yongfeng to attack Tantou and approach the north of Donggu. At the same time, the 19th Route Army also sent a part of its troops to bypass Xingguo and join Luo's army from Taihe to put pressure on the west of Donggu from Chengjiang Tiantu. Chiang Tingwen led the 9th and 23rd Divisions as a reserve force at the southeastern border. After the above deployments were completed, the general attack order was issued on the 23rd. A total of more than 200,000 troops were mobilized. When they advanced to the vicinity of the communist nests, the Huang Gonglue and Lin Biao bandit armies took advantage of the dangerous terrain and pre-built fortifications to resist the Communist Suppression Army from high ground with firearms. The Communist Suppression Army fought one after another. The battles of Longgang and Luokou were extremely fierce. The sounds of machine guns, cannons, rifles, and grenades were mixed together, like the big and small cannons of the New Year. However, the Communist Suppression Army's air force soared through the sky, using message bags to report the location of the bandit's main force and the direction of advance. The fortifications of the communist nests were also bombed and destroyed by the planes. The Red Bandits suffered heavy casualties. By the 25th and 26th, the left wing first recaptured the communist nests of Huangpi, Xiaopu, Dongshan, and Luokou, killing countless bandits. The bodies of the bandits were strewn everywhere, most of whom were peasant bandits. On the right wing, the Li Yunjie units of Shangguan Yunxiang's forces in the Third Route Army first defeated about one division of Huang Gonglue's forces and occupied Shaxi. Then, they suddenly and unexpectedly infiltrated from Xiagu Cangqian to the back of the bandit camp in light clothing. At this time, Cai Tingkai led the First Army Corps directly from Shanggu to Longgang, and taking advantage of the victory, moved westward with lightning speed and captured Donggu at 1:00 PM on the 27th. When the bandits occupying the nest, such as Wu Zhonghao's pseudo-army, came out to resist, they engaged Cai's division in a close-quarters battle. When the two sides were fighting hand-to-hand, the teams of the Communist Suppression Army surrounding Donggu rushed in like surging tides. Moreover, the key points and contact points of Donggu were cut off by the Communist Suppression Army. The Red Bandits were unable to respond to each other and were completely annihilated. According to news from the Forward Headquarters, a total of more than 30,000 Red Army peasant bandits, militia, and spear teams, both male and female, were captured in the Battle of Donggu. 14,000 to 15,000 土 guns, rifles, and broken and miscellaneous firearms, as well as other weapons, important documents, and oil, salt, rice, and grain robbed by the Red Bandits, were seized. The various pseudo-organs of the Red Bandits were immediately destroyed without remainder, and the hostages who had been kidnapped were released. Also, the Forward Headquarters reported that in the battles of Huangpi and other places, in addition to countless bandits killed, at least 50,000 hostages were released, peasant bandits were disbanded, and bandits were captured successively. Although a small number of bandits fled to Xingguo and Yudu, trying to escape from Ruijin and Xiangzhou, the Communist Suppression Army had made careful arrangements in advance and planned to intercept and wipe them out in Gulonggang and other places. The three prisoner-of-war camps in Linchuan, Ji'an, and Nanchang are being actively prepared for establishment by the Party and Government Council to actively receive the wounded soldiers. Corpses are being buried, and the Red Cross teams sent from Shanghai have set off to Nanfeng, Ji'an, Ningdu, and Donggu to treat the wounded soldiers. (July 28)

Although we are working with Shanghai gentry to raise funds for relief, we fear that repeated calls for help will not achieve significant results. Such an extraordinary disaster cannot be solved with a small amount of funds, and it is even more important to provide urgent relief quickly to save the dying people. Wandering at midnight, we do not know what to do. This would allow the people to live and the foundation of the country to be secure. I am eagerly awaiting your instructions. We implore your approval and prompt implementation. This would be a merciful act. Furthermore, we still hope that the Disaster Relief Reserve Fund Law can be implemented as soon as possible, so that we can be prepared for any eventuality. This is jointly stated.

He Chengjun

Reports to the National Government on the Hubei Disaster

▲ Requests the Relief Committee to Allocate Huge Sums for Relief

▲ Wuhan Announces Special Martial Law

Hankou Correspondence: He Chengjun, Chairman of the Hubei Provincial Government, considering the extraordinarily severe floods in the province, specifically reported the disaster situation to the National Government and the Executive Yuan on the 29th, requesting the Relief Committee to promptly allocate huge sums for relief. The telegram reads: I have investigated that since the beginning of summer, Hubei Province has experienced continuous rain for many days, coupled with sudden mountain floods. At the same time, the Yangtze and Han Rivers have risen, and the embankments have collapsed, causing the water to overflow and inundate the area. Even areas known for their high elevation have suffered from excessive rainfall and accumulated water, resulting in massive flooding. In addition, the season coincides with the hottest period of the year, and the rice and wheat have been submerged. The fields and livestock have all been swept away by the floods, turning the world of humans into a hellish scene, with cries of distress heard everywhere. Evil dragons and sea monsters wreak havoc, with raging waves reaching the sky. The suffering of those displaced and the tragedy of families torn apart are difficult to describe in words and are rarely seen in recent years. In recent days, we have repeatedly received reports from various places, such as Mianyang, Hanchuan, Hanyang, Huanggang, Yunmeng, Qianjiang, Xiaogan, and Jiayu counties, that the embankments have been submerged. Reports of disaster caused by continuous rain have come from counties such as Songzi, Xianning, Shishou, Yingcheng, and Qishui. Reports of mountain floods destroying fields and gardens have come from counties such as Luotian. The Yangtze River is currently overflowing, and although the heavy rain has stopped, the sky is covered with dark clouds, and we do not know how many more disaster reports will continue to come in. Even in Wuhan, such as Hualou in Hankou, the Chenjiaji area in various special districts, and the area outside Wushengmen in Nanhu, Wuchang, have all become swamps, with no end in sight. The residents are distressed, and travel is difficult. There is a danger of the cooking smoke ceasing, and every step is met with the叹息 of drowning. As for the counties that have not been flooded, they are suffering from banditry, and people are scattered in all directions. People from neighboring counties seeking refuge have no way to find food and no place to live in this disaster, and their cries of sorrow are unbearable to hear. The future consequences will be even greater. In addition to ordering the Civil Affairs Department to select capable officials to go to various districts to conduct thorough inspections, provide careful support, and supervise the Water Conservancy Bureau, Wuhan, and various counties and cities to find ways to drain the accumulated water, strictly prevent bandits from taking advantage of the situation, and convene gentry and merchants to discuss providing urgent relief, I am reporting the extraordinary severity of this year's flood in Hubei Province to Your Excellency for review and reference. I also beg that the Central Relief Committee be ordered to promptly allocate huge sums for relief and send them to Hubei for disaster relief, to extend benevolence and provide peace to the poor and suffering. I am writing this telegram with the utmost urgency and eagerness for instructions.

The Garrison Headquarters also announced special martial law on the 29th, effective immediately, due to the flooding of Wuhan streets, the clustering of citizens, and the fear of troublemakers causing disturbances. The announcement is as follows: Announcement: It has been investigated that Wuhan streets have been flooded for days, and order is quite chaotic. Troublemakers are taking advantage of the situation, endangering peace and security, which is a cause for concern and must be strictly prevented. With the approval of the General Headquarters of the Army, Navy, and Air Force, special martial law will be implemented. Traffic will be cut off at night. The streets of the three districts of Hankou, Wuchang, and Hanyang, as well as the outer edges of the garrison area, will be completely closed to traffic from 11:00 PM to 5:00 AM the next morning. (Omission) In addition, the following temporary warning has been issued to the sentries: Do not neglect your duties due to the flooding of the streets, and be especially vigilant than usual. Shops that have been flooded should close early. This is a serious announcement. (July 30)

Hankou Juxingcheng Bank Robbed

▲ Banking Association Requests Protection from Authorities

Hankou Correspondence: The Hankou Juxingcheng Bank was robbed by bandits on the 25th. The Hankou Banking Association specifically sent letters to the General Headquarters of the Army, Navy, and Air Force, the Hubei Provincial Government, the Wuhan Garrison Headquarters, the Hankou Municipal Government, the Hankou Third Special District Municipal Administration, and the Hankou Municipal Public Security Bureau, requesting prompt measures to maintain law and order. The letter reads: Robbery in broad daylight, endangering law and order, causing panic on the streets, everyone is trembling with fear. We respectfully request that measures be taken to protect the situation to reassure merchants and maintain local peace. We respectfully report that, according to a letter from our member Juxingcheng Bank, today (July 25th) at 11:25 AM, while the bank was open for business, six bandits suddenly mixed in with the customers at the main entrance. One of them was tall with a slightly pockmarked face, speaking with a northern accent. He first snatched over two thousand yuan in banknotes from a remitter, brandished a handgun, and forbade anyone from making a sound. At the same time, the other bandits were each holding guns to intimidate people, one watching the telephone, two patrolling outside the counter, and the remaining two rushing into the counter, heading straight for the cashier's office, pointing guns at them, and then using the bags they brought to pack up over four thousand yuan in banknotes that were placed on the counter. They then leisurely left. At that time, a collector from the Banque de l'Indochine had exchanged eighty yuan in banknotes and was robbed as he was walking to the main entrance. The bandits left in succession, heading towards the Yiyuan area and disappearing. Our bank had pressed the alarm bell when it was being robbed to notify the authorities, but the police and soldiers did not arrive. It was only later discovered that the alarm bell was broken and ineffective. After the incident, we reported it to the Special Third District Administration and the Hankou Municipal Public Security Bureau by telephone, but the bandits had already disappeared. In addition to separately reporting this matter and requesting the arrest and punishment of the bandits, we are first informing the Banking Association for your information. Juxingcheng Bank is located at a wharf, close to the former Hualou, a busy transportation hub in the port area. It was midday, the weather was clear, and there was a constant flow of pedestrians and many patrolling soldiers and police. The bandits dared to commit a robbery with guns in broad daylight, acting calmly and unhurriedly, showing no fear in their hearts, treating the soldiers and police as if they were nothing, and disrupting the law and order of the city. If this trend continues, the consequences will be unimaginable. The damage to Juxingcheng Bank may seem like an isolated incident, but there are numerous banks and shops in Hankou, and similar dangers could occur anywhere and at any time. Moreover, banks handle cash and banknotes, with amounts often reaching tens of thousands of yuan, which is common. Customers make payments and receipts, and there is no fixed schedule. In this atmosphere of terror, we do not know where to find protection. All the banks in our association were deeply surprised to hear the news of the robbery of Juxingcheng Bank in broad daylight. We have jointly discussed and believe that everyone is in danger, and the situation on the streets is unpredictable. If we do not take measures to protect the situation, we will not be able to reassure merchants and maintain local peace. In addition to the bank reporting the matter and requesting the arrest and punishment of the bandits, which should be done by the bank, the incident is so strange that we cannot remain silent. We must detail the dangerous situation and respectfully inform Your Excellency of the situation. We beg that Your Bureau investigate and promptly take measures to maintain law and order, so that such robberies can be eliminated from now on, and the city's businesses can be safe. We also ask for your instructions to be followed. With utmost urgency and eagerness for instructions, we respectfully present this to the Hankou Banking Association, July 25th, 20th year [of the Republic].

Wu Peifu Travels to Chengdu via Shunqing

▲ Wu gives moral lectures everywhere

▲ Li Qixiang Provides Travel Expenses of Ten Thousand Yuan

Shunqing Correspondence: Wu Peifu arrived in Shunqing from Suilai a few days ago, on June 25th. He stayed for eight days before proceeding to the provincial capital. During his stay in Shunqing, he had earnest conversations with Li Qixiang. The following is a record of his passage through Shunqing and his journey to the provincial capital:

Wu arrived in Shunqing on June 25th, and that evening Li Qixiang hosted a lavish banquet to welcome Wu. On the 26th, the Border Defense Army also arranged a theatrical performance at a theater to welcome him. On the 27th, Xiong Yuzhang of the 23rd Division invited Wu to a feast at Ganlu Temple. Wu's son was always by his side, accompanying him whether he was sightseeing or attending banquets. On the 28th, Wu had some free time, but there were too many visitors to the 行辕, making it difficult to meet them all individually. He specifically invited representatives from various Shunqing government agencies, legal entities, and gentry to attend a lecture at the Guoshan Theater. After the crowd gathered, Wu, wearing an old-fashioned army cap, a long gown, and a black waistcoat, ascended the stage. After a few words of self-deprecation, he spoke about filial piety, brotherly love, loyalty, trustworthiness, propriety, righteousness, integrity, and shame, emphasizing the two characters of morality to encourage everyone. After the speech, he distributed copies of his book "Following One's Duty," with an attached letter, to each person. After distributing the books, he repeated his exhortations several times before everyone dispersed. On the 29th, leaders from the Nanchong County Bureau and local government agencies and legal entities hosted a banquet for Wu at the Guoshan Theater. Wu, his son, Li Qixiang, Xiong Yuzhang, Wang Boyuan, He Zhanru, Liu Hanxiong, Li Qingting, Ye Jishi, Yang Duanwu, Fan Yingshi, Chen Shaotang, Zhang Ximin, and about one hundred other senior military officers attended. Wu, wearing casual clothes and a hat, sat alone in the center seat, with his son below him and only Li Qixiang and Xiong Yuzhang accompanying him on both sides. The other personnel were seated on the left and right sides. The tables were surrounded by Wu's guards, all holding knives, guns, and grenades, numbering about three hundred people, standing and waiting, with no one daring to sit down without permission. After the performance began, the first play was "Chang'e Flying to the Moon," and Wu rewarded it with one hundred yuan. Li Qixiang requested "Battle of Yongzhou" and rewarded it with fifty yuan. Xiong Yuzhang requested "Gathering of Heroes" and rewarded it with forty yuan. Other brigade commanders requested many plays, and the banquet did not end until after midnight. On the 30th, Wu, about to leave Shunqing, hosted a banquet for leaders from various Nanchong government agencies and legal entities at the Shunqing Guoshan Theater as a farewell memento. Around 4:00 PM, the guests arrived one after another. Before the performance began, Wu gave a brief speech, first expressing his gratitude to everyone, and then talking about how the world and people's hearts are too corrupt in modern times, and that it is impossible to govern the world without restoring people's hearts. To restore people's hearts, we must emphasize morality, promote propriety and righteousness, and teach the people filial piety and brotherly love. Someone in the audience asked about military and political affairs, but Wu immediately declined, refusing to discuss them. Wu originally planned to leave Shunqing and head west on July 1st, but postponed his departure until the 3rd because there were still matters to be arranged in Shunqing. However, on the evening before his departure (2nd), he went to the Border Defense Army Headquarters to bid farewell to Li Qixiang. Li Qixiang prepared a farewell banquet, and there was a lingering reluctance during the banquet. After the banquet, Li ordered someone to deliver ten thousand yuan as travel expenses to strengthen his journey. After Wu received it, he sent an aide-de-camp to Li's headquarters to express his gratitude. Xiong Yuzhang, the acting commander of the 23rd Division, also went to Wu's 行辕 on the evening of the 2nd to bid him farewell, and presented him with one thousand yuan in 現欵 and various local products from Nanchong. Wu accepted everything. On the morning of the 3rd, after 5:00 AM, the Border Defense Army and the 23rd Division prepared fifty pack animals and two hundred and fifty porters for Wu, all gathered at Wu's 行辕. After the luggage was loaded, they set off. The whole city was covered with flags, and there were many people at the train station outside the Sanjiao Temple to see him off. Wu, wearing a blue silk robe, a black gauze waistcoat, and a soft felt hat, traveled to the station by car with his wife, Mrs. Zhang, and his son, and then changed to a sedan chair because the road to Tongchuan had not yet been built. Wang Hongen, who had served as a brigade commander in the Northwest Army and had been stationed in Guangyuan for a long time, also traveled with Wu. Li Qixiang, Xiong Yuzhang, He Zhanru, Liu Hanxiong, Fan Yingshi, Pang Yuqing, and Long Huanzhang, as well as the heads of local agencies and the Nanchong County Bureau, all went outside the city to see him off. There were about three hundred pistol-wielding soldiers escorting the luggage ahead, Wu and his wife led their son and Wang Hongen, as well as Wu's senior officers, about seventy people in total, and fifty bodyguards, followed. The grenade team and the remaining four or five hundred officers marched at the rear. As he was about to depart, Wu took off his hat and nodded goodbye to Li Qixiang and the other well-wishers.

Since Wu's arrival in Shunqing, there has been a banquet every day, and visitors have been thronging the streets, almost leaving him no free time. Moreover, Wu, as a Grand Marshal, was accompanied by hundreds of people for every move he made. When he walked, the streets were blocked, and when he stayed, the houses were full. The grenade team and the bodyguards, numbering about seventy or eighty people, closely followed him at all times. During banquets, the streets he passed through were extensively guarded in advance, and pedestrians were prohibited from passing. Then, he would travel by car. The same was true when he returned to the 行辕 after the banquet. Therefore, after Wu stayed in Shunqing for several days, the military and political authorities and local people began to feel a little annoyed. When Wu was scheduled to go to the provincial capital, the Border Defense Headquarters specially prepared three hundred catties of pork, ten jars of fine wine, and one thousand silver dollars to reward Wu's entourage. All of this shows the friendship between Li Qixiang and Wu.

Report from the Korean Consulate General's Office on the Incheon Riot

Report: I have investigated that the cause of this Korean riot was the Korean Daily News' propaganda about the Wanbaoshan Incident, issuing a special edition (which has been reported to the Consulate General), fabricating facts. It began at 2:00 AM on the 3rd of this month. While Wenhe was sound asleep, he was suddenly awakened by a servant, who claimed that someone had urgently reported that dozens of Koreans were throwing stones at Chinese food shops, barbershops, and restaurants in the outer district of Incheon, breaking many windows and light bulbs. He requested that the police station be notified by telephone for protection. Because the matter involved violence, Wenhe immediately got out of bed. In addition to notifying the police station to send police officers quickly, he went by car to investigate because it was raining heavily and the road was far. He confirmed that the Qingyuntang barbershop and Yongdelou restaurant were indeed damaged in the outer district. He immediately returned to the office. By dawn, rumors of a Korean riot were spreading, and僑民 were flocking to Chinatown to seek refuge. Fearing a major disaster, Wenhe rushed to the police station around 8:00 AM and met with Director Dongchuan, asking him to prohibit the newspaper from spreading its exaggerated stories and to take steps to prevent a repeat of the tragedy of 1927. After returning to the office, he also called Consul General Zhang to ask the Governor-General to order police stations in various places to provide effective protection until 6:00 PM. Koreans gathered in large numbers at the railway bridge in the outer district to give speeches. Upon hearing the news, Wenhe immediately called the police station to stop them and accompanied Chairman Chuan of the Chamber of Commerce and Director Dongchuan to inspect the area. Seeing that the Koreans on the street were gradually dispersing, he felt quite relieved. Unexpectedly, around 8:00 PM, Koreans gathered again, numbering over three thousand, and launched a large-scale riot. The whole city was in chaos. Chinese men and women fled, and the doors and windows of Chinese businesses were smashed. The police could not stop them. Wenhe accompanied Chairman Chuan of the Chamber of Commerce to the police station to request armed action to suppress the riot. The director refused to send troops because he had not received orders from the Provincial Office. The rioters then formed a group and attacked Chinatown. Fortunately, our僑民 defended together and prevented them from entering. The rioters retreated and threw stones at Chinese shops along the way, looting and discarding goods. Many僑民 were injured that night, but no one was killed. The larger shops of Chinese merchants in the inner and outer districts did not suffer significant losses. By dawn, the rioters had dispersed somewhat, but there were rumors that the Koreans would attack Chinatown on the evening of the 4th, and some Koreans who were friendly with Chinese also called to advise them to take temporary shelter to avoid danger. As a result, everyone was frightened and at a loss, and they came to the office to report the situation. Wenhe urgently reported the situation to Consul General Zhang by telephone, requesting the Governor-General to send additional armed police to Incheon for protection. At the same time, he rushed to the police station to question the director, stating that since he had declared that he was responsible for protection, why could he not stop the rioters? Did he have the ability to provide protection? He asked for a clear answer so that he could plan accordingly. The director replied that there were not many police officers here and that there might be inadequate protection outside the government office. However, the Koreans were only throwing stones and beating people, and there would be no major incidents. He hoped that the Chinese would not resist, so as not to make it impossible to maintain order. He would take full responsibility for the lives and property of the Chinese. At 4:00 PM, Consul Zhang Mao came to Incheon and addressed the僑民, saying that the Governor-General had agreed to send additional police officers and asked everyone to be at ease. Later, he accompanied Wenhe to the police station to meet with the director and asked him if he was confident in maintaining law and order. The director still said that he was fully responsible. Before leaving, Consul General Zhang told the director that the lives and property of the four thousand Chinese侨民 in Incheon were all in his hands. He replied that he was fully responsible. Around 9:00 PM, it was reported that the Koreans had gathered again in the outer district, beating drums and gathering a crowd of about five thousand people, and had begun to riot, wielding wooden sticks, iron bars, knives, and axes, searching and attacking everywhere. All the Chinese shops in the inner and outer districts were broken open by the rioters using freight cars, and the telephone and electric wires were cut with knives and axes. Goods were looted and discarded, and the streets were in a terrible state. Finally, cloth and silk were hung on trees or wrapped around telephone poles and wires. The Koreans rioted in front, and the police followed behind, completely losing the ability to protect. The whole city was in a state of panic, like a battlefield. Calls for help from各僑用 telephone poured in. At that time, the Chinese侨民 in Incheon were in danger of being completely wiped out. Upon receiving the report, we immediately telegraphed Consul General Zhang, asking him to negotiate with the Governor-General and send a large number of soldiers and police to Incheon for assistance. At the same time, we telegraphed the Incheon police station, asking them to provide effective protection for the lives and property of all the Chinese僑民. Around 3:00 AM on the 5th, seventeen armed police officers and gendarmes from the capital arrived. The police were also armed. Seeing the situation was not good, they fired two shots into the air, and the rioters retreated. They did not enter Chinatown because of the heavy police presence, so Chinatown was spared. In the early morning, the僑民 widely rumored that many people had been killed by the Koreans in the outer district and in the Zhuan area outside the government office. Wenhe accompanied Chairman Chuan of the Chamber of Commerce to search for them and inspect the devastation in the inner and outer districts. He took photos on the spot as evidence. He also went to the Changyili mountain stone ranch near Zhuan and found that Lian Kuishan and Li Houji from the outer district had been beaten to death, a total of two people. There were also two people still alive, Lu Huanxin and Wang Youzhi, who were hired by a car to send to the Muze Surgical Hospital, hoping to avoid death, but according to the doctor, they may be disabled. They are currently still in the hospital. A cargo truck was urgently hired to transport僑民 from far and near to Chinatown for refuge, a total of 1,500 people. The two deceased were dissected by Wenhe together with Di, an inspector (prosecutor) from the Incheon branch of the 京城检事局, at the Incheon Quarantine Station, and then buried by the Chamber of Commerce. There were also more than twenty people with minor injuries. On the morning of the 5th, about four thousand rioters gathered around Chinatown, attempting to attack in front of the Incheon Government Office, which was less than half a mile from Chinatown. Fortunately, the police dispersed them with cavalry. In the outer district, they set fire to one place. The 本办事处, the Chamber of Commerce, and the school had sheltered about 3,600 refugees in the past three days. Things have gradually calmed down since the 6th, but the侨民 are all like frightened birds. Therefore, from the 6th to yesterday, more than 8,000 people have taken the Chinese 利通号轮船 and the Japanese 共同丸 from Incheon to return to China. Currently, about two hundred people are still taking refuge in the Chinese primary school, etc. Later, Consul General Zhang came to Incheon to express his condolences and investigate.

According to investigations, the direct losses in Incheon alone are about 90,000 日金. The indirect losses are currently being investigated in detail. I have collected the details of this riot in Incheon. I hope that you will consider it. Chiang Wenhe, Director of the Incheon Office of the Consulate General of the Republic of China in Korea, July 20.

Local Correspondence

Songjiang

Meeting of the Land Tax Investigation Committee: The county government and the Finance Bureau of this county previously received an order from the Department of Finance to organize a Land Tax Investigation Committee. The former county magistrate appointed committee members, and the committee was organized according to regulations. Yesterday (the 30th), the third meeting of the committee was held, presided over by County Magistrate Shen. Matters discussed included: (1) Land registration, the revised detailed rules have been issued and should be followed. However, the previous work was handled by the district chiefs. Now, how should it be handled? Resolved: The Finance Bureau shall entrust the district chiefs to handle it conscientiously. (2) The chairman submitted a public letter from the Songqing Jinsha Land Official Property Branch, based on laws and regulations, proposing four points for resolution. Resolved: (A) Handle according to Article 1 of the "Measures for Supplementing Grain and Increasing Taxes on Land with No Grain Due to Wasteland." (B) If there are reports, the Finance Bureau should instruct the compilation of books or the township police to verify the numbers before processing. (C) Handle according to Articles 5 and 6 of the "Measures for Supplementing Grain and Increasing Taxes on Land with No Grain Due to Wasteland." (D) Handle according to regulations and mutually investigate.

Appointment of Charitable Board Members: The board members of the Charity Board of the seven counties formerly under Songjiang Prefecture are appointed by the county magistrate of this county after each county nominates candidates according to regulations. It has been found that the terms of the board members of Nanhui and Shanghai counties have expired. Gong Yuanben has been nominated by Nanhui and Shen Zhou has been nominated by Shanghai to succeed them. County Magistrate Shen has approved the nominations and sent letters of appointment. The terms of the board members of Songjiang County who have completed their terms have also been extended by County Magistrate Shen to ensure familiarity with the work.

Guan Daming's Appeal in the Case of Seducing a Minor Girl: Guan Daming, the owner of the Gaodi Western Firm shoe store on Jing'an Temple Road in Shanghai, was sentenced by the Shanghai District Court in the case of seducing and cohabiting with Chen Xuanying, a minor girl from Suzhou. Guan was convicted of raping a girl under the age of sixteen and sentenced to three years and six months of imprisonment. Guan disagreed with the verdict and appealed to the High Court. Yesterday (the 31st), the Shanghai District Court ordered the police to escort Guan to Suzhou and send him to the High Court Detention Center on Siqian Street to await interrogation.

Appeal Judgment in the Zheng-Su Divorce Case: The divorce appeal case between Zheng Su Xuewu, a woman from Shanghai, and Zheng Shaopo, the manager of a Norwegian shipping company, was pronounced by the High Court yesterday (the 31st). The original judgment regarding ornaments and litigation costs was changed. The respondent should return two gold bracelets and two gold rings to the appellant. The appellant shall bear nineteen-twentieths of the remaining appeal costs, and the respondent shall bear one-twentieth.

Water Police Capture Two Kidnappers: The 11th Squad of the 3rd District of the Water Public Security Bureau stationed in Fanhuangdai Township captured Shen Jizhang (33 years old) and Shen Jigen (37 years old), two brothers from Chao Lake, Anhui, who were bandits who kidnapped a man named Shen from Shenjia Village, a village with residents from both north and south China. They were sent to the district headquarters for interrogation on the 31st.

Telegram Urging Shanghai Merchants to Stop Importing Japanese Goods: The Economic Severance Committee of the Wuxian Merchants Association, based on the telegram from the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce, has been established and is actively proceeding, starting with the investigation and registration of Japanese goods. However, since the source of Japanese goods in Suzhou is mainly Shanghai, a telegram was sent to the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce yesterday (the 31st), requesting that it lead all merchants to voluntarily stop importing Japanese goods to eliminate the root cause and better protect the inland commercial sector.

Wuxi

Countywide Mass Meeting to Oppose Japan and Aid Overseas Chinese: The Executive Committee of the Wuxi County Party Headquarters convened a countywide mass meeting to oppose Japan and aid overseas Chinese yesterday morning (the 31st) at the public sports field. A memorial service was held for the deceased overseas Chinese compatriots, and eight measures for aiding the distressed overseas Chinese compatriots were resolved.

Another Case of Opening a Coffin for Re-examination: Ding Ruqing, a houseboat resident from Tan D渡 Bridge outside the South Gate, had a daughter named Gendi, who married Cheng Wengan from Yancheng. On the afternoon of May 28th of this year, Cheng Wengan's body was suddenly found on the riverbank of Tan渡 Bridge. Prosecutor Zhu of the County Court, accompanied by a coroner, went to examine the body and confirmed that he had died by falling into the river. However, the deceased's elder brothers, Wenpei and Wenhan, refused to accept this and went to Ding Ruqing's house, dragging Ding to the Public Security Bureau, claiming that Wengan did not die by falling into the river but was beaten to death by Ding Ruqing and thrown into the river because his wife, Gendi, was unfaithful. Ding Ruqing denied this and was transferred to the County Court for questioning. However, each party maintained their previous statements. Ding Ruqing, his wife Xiao, and daughter Gendi have been detained until now without a resolution. The Cheng Wenpei brothers expressed distrust of Prosecutor Zhu's examination and entrusted a lawyer to appeal to the High Court Prosecutor's Office, which approved a re-examination of the body. Yesterday, Prosecutor Du issued a summons to the Cheng Wenpei and Wenhan brothers and interrogated Ding Ruqing, Ding Xiao, and Ding Gendi, who were in custody, before submitting a report to the High Court for review.

Re-election of Representatives to the Second Provincial Congress: The Executive Committee of this county, because the Second Jiangsu Provincial Congress will be held in Zhenjiang on August 15th, with the deadline approaching, ordered the sub-branches in each district to elect representatives to the preliminary election of provincial representatives. A re-election was held at 3:00 PM yesterday in the auditorium of the County Party Headquarters. The Provincial Party Rectification Committee specially sent Instructor Chen Kanghe to supervise the election. As a result of the election, Hu Nianqian, Li Tiping, Ji Pu, and Qiu Youzhen were elected as representatives. After the election was completed, the ballots for the preliminary election of national representatives were opened, and Zhang Renjie was elected as a representative to the preliminary election of the Fourth National Congress.

Changzhou

Large Number of Vagrants Escape from the Reformatory: The Wuyi Vagrant Reformatory, which houses about ninety-seven vagrants, who usually do weaving and other crafts, closed the main gate of the vagrant residences at 8:00 PM on the 30th. Suddenly, a noise was heard inside the gate. After the patrol chief opened the lock and tried to enter to mediate, the vagrants, armed with tile bowls and wooden sticks, rushed forward and beat the patrol chief and patrolmen. They then rushed out to the north. The gate guards were unable to stop them. The incident was reported to the Public Security Bureau for assistance in the pursuit. Those who escaped were chased back, but after a headcount, it was found that thirty-two vagrants, including Yuan Bingquan, had escaped. Director Zhao Yonghuai reported to the county government, which immediately closed the city to search. Only four or five people had been captured by late at night. The search is still ongoing today (the 31st).

Notorious Bandit Qin Erger Captured: Qin Erger, a notorious bandit from Wuyi, was recently found by Captain Ni Gusheng to be hiding in Shanghai. He took detectives to Shanghai to investigate. After half a month, they encountered Qin Erger behind the Great World. He notified the police on duty to arrest him and hand him over to the District Court.

A detective was sent back to Changzhou on the 30th to report to County Magistrate Zhang, who immediately prepared a document to be transferred to Shanghai and handed Qin Erger over to Changzhou for legal proceedings on the 31st.

Nantong

Thorough Investigation of the Body Dumping Case of the "Dahe" Ship: The "Dahe" ship of the Dada Company's Shanghai-Yangzhou line unloaded an injured corpse at Tianshenggang and then took it upstream. After someone reported it, the corpse was allegedly dumped into the river. The county government, believing that Tang Ruiquan, the director of the port Public Security Bureau, had unclear procedures and was suspected of accepting bribes, has dismissed him from his post pending a thorough investigation by the court. The High Court has designated the Zhenjiang District Court to handle the case. The entire file has been sent to Zhenjiang. The Nantong County Court has received a letter from the Zhenjiang District Court, forwarding it to the Public Security Bureau, stating that since the Dada Company claimed that the corpse was taken away by the corpse's nephew, Li Yifu, they should indicate the burial address so that personnel can be sent to verify the truth.

Methods for Raising Bank Protection Funds: The collapse of the riverbank in Nantong is becoming more severe. The local financial resources for handling bank protection projects are limited. Appeals have been made to the province. The provincial government has approved the allocation of funds to subsidize the project from the income from the increased tax on reed fields, and has approved the bank protection association's request to collect an additional 3.5% tax per mu on land tax for bank protection. The total cost of the fundamental project is estimated at 300,000 yuan. The shortfall will be covered by issuing local public bonds.

Severe Flooding in the Surrounding Villages: Severe flooding has occurred in Tongyi. Although the gates and culverts of the rivers and seas have been opened, the agricultural land and houses in the surrounding villages are still underwater. Agricultural products have rotted, and the disaster is severe. Disaster victims in each district have requested relief from the county government.

Yangzhou

Capture of Fugitive Xu Maorong: Wei Ting, the captain of the police brigade in this county, secretly dispatched a detective team to Zishizi Street outside the Dongguan City a few days ago and captured the fugitive Xu Guozhang (i.e., Xu Maorong). According to the suspect's confession during the preliminary interrogation, he had partnered with others to rob the Huo Jiaqiao Security Corps and other places in June of last year, receiving five yuan in stolen goods. The team presented the already captured accomplice, He Dezheng, for confrontation, and the details of the confession matched. The confession was recorded, and the suspect was handed over to the county government for interrogation and punishment.

Order for Local Militia to be Placed Under the Command of the Pacification Director: Zhang Zhijiang, the Pacification Director of Jiangsu, presented a request to the General Headquarters because the pacification forces were insufficient for distribution. Yesterday, it was reported that the headquarters sent a return telegram to the office stating that the request was granted to temporarily place the Jiangsu militia under command due to insufficient pacification forces. In addition to sending telegrams to Chairman Ye of the Jiangsu Provincial Government and the Security Department for compliance, this was urgently reported.

Zhenjiang

All Shops Prohibited from Transporting Japanese Goods Anymore: The Provincial Propaganda Committee has recently learned that Zhenjiang merchants are actively transporting Japanese goods amidst the anti-Japanese movement, seeking profit from the opportunity. This behavior is not what any citizen with a conscience should do. Yesterday, the committee sent a letter to the Chamber of Commerce, stipulating that all shops in Zhenjiang must not transport Japanese goods after August 1st. If any violations are discovered, they will be confiscated.

Ye Chucang's Second Son Drowns While Swimming in the River: Yesterday afternoon at around 4:00 PM, the second son of Chairman Ye of the Provincial Government first played basketball at the public playground of the Civil Affairs Department. Because of the hot weather, he and the eldest son of the Director of the Civil Affairs Department, Hu Pu'an, and four clerks from the fourth section of the Civil Affairs Department went to the riverbank of the Zhongzheng Bridge in the South Gate to swim. All four entered the water at the same time. After a while, the Civil Affairs Department clerk and the eldest son of Hu could not see Chairman Ye's second son and the Wang clerk in the water and knew that they had drowned. The Provincial Government immediately reported to the government and sent laborers to salvage the bodies. The two were hooked up and retrieved. Chairman Ye has four sons, this being his second son, who was only sixteen years old. At that time, Chairman Ye had gone to Beijing on official business. The Provincial Government reported to Beijing that evening.

Jiangyin

Relief for Flood Disaster in Qingsi Two Villages: The Tenth District, Qingsi River Two villages, are located in a low-lying area. Since suffering from continuous rain and disaster, the flood has swept across, and the farmland has been submerged. Those who cannot be rescued account for four or five out of ten. The two villages specially recommended representatives Wu Fengnian, Zhou Zhonghui, Feng Jiaxi, etc., to the County Government on the 28th to visit County Magistrate Peng and request relief. County Magistrate Peng replied: (1) In terms of remedies, the County Government will send a letter to the Wuxi Farmers Bank to raise huge sums of money to be lent to each household. (2) In terms of disaster relief, the county will send a fast telegram to the Provincial Flood Relief Committee to allocate funds for relief. The representatives then resigned.

RugaO

Xuejia Kiln Township Chief Brutally Murdered by Bandits: Xue Hanqing, the township chief of Xuejia Kiln Township in the Zhentao District of Rugao, went to Zhujiabu on business at 8:00 PM on the 27th. On his way home, when he reached the west end of Xuejia Kiln, suddenly many Red Bandits came face to face, holding guns. When the township chief saw this situation, he jumped into the river to escape. However, the bandits also went into the water with guns and chased him, causing Township Chief Xue to be brutally shot. When the local people heard the news, they flew to report to the county police and the Security Corps stationed in the area to track down and suppress the bandits, but they had already disappeared without a trace.

Bandits Active in Caolan Embankment: In the Caolan Embankment area of Zhentao Township in this county, more than 20 bandits suddenly came on the night of the 27th, holding guns, intending to kill the township chief and deputy of the area. Fortunately, they did not encounter them. The bandits turned back halfway and encountered Wang Mao, a notorious bandit from the area who had surrendered, who was captured and shot. It is reported that the bandits who came to the embankment this time were led by Yu Xian, a notorious bandit from Fenghuo Port, who came here to operate.

Gaoyou

Grain Boat Robbed at Huajiatan: Wu Guozong, a grain merchant from Jiangba Town in Xuyi County, loaded a boat of miscellaneous grains in that area a few days ago and came to Gaoyou to sell it. However, yesterday morning (the 26th), when he arrived at the Huajiatan area, he suddenly encountered a boat. Four bandits jumped out, each holding a gun, and ordered the boat to stop. They jumped onto Wu's boat and searched extensively, robbing a self-defense gun and more than 200 yuan.

Sudden Increase in River Water and All Alarmed to Secure the Dyke: In this county yesterday at about 4:00 PM, a sudden light rain fell and a southwest wind rose, causing the water level of the canal to suddenly rise from 1.7 zhang to 1.78 zhang. The west dyke was completely submerged by water. Residents living on the west dyke moved to the east dyke. The lake and river were connected and indistinguishable, a vast expanse of water. At 9:00 PM, a low dyke at the Jieganting section outside the South Gate suddenly overflowed, which was extremely dangerous. The alarm was immediately sounded to secure the dyke and raise the height of the dyke body. Fortunately, there was no problem. The authorities in this county, because the water level was increasing and there was a danger of the dyke breaking, hired workers overnight to block the Touzhakou and the river mouths along the river, preparing to open the dams for drainage. However, more than 1,000 farmers in Xinghua, seeing that Gaoyou intended to open the dams, became very panicked. They gathered at the Touzhakou and river mouths, refusing to allow them to be blocked. There has been no result yet. Fortunately, the sky has cleared today and the southwest wind has stopped, and the water has receded to 1.75 zhang. It is hoped that there will be no more strong winds and rain, so that each dam can be preserved until it is opened after autumn.

Xinghua

Xinghua Legal Organizations Petition to Protect the Dams: Representatives of various legal organizations in Xinghua, Ruan Zhongmei and Ruan Yicheng, presented a petition to the Provincial Government, the Ministry of Interior, and the Huai River Guidance Association, stating that they had lived in Xinghua County, Jiangsu Province, for generations and knew the water conditions of the upper and lower rivers. In years of severe flooding, the five dams in Gaoyou County that return to the sea are never lightly opened until after the beginning of autumn. There are precedents to follow for decades. A telegram was received from the Xinghua County Legal Organizations stating that the old practice of opening the dams is after autumn, and before autumn there will be no harvest, and they urgently await the calls of various key officials for help, to protect as much as possible, etc. The five dams are named as returning to the sea, but in fact they are far from the sea. The water flowing down from the dams is no different from harming the neighbor. Now, with continuous rain causing disaster, spreading across several provinces, and various counties in Jiangbei also suffering, if one of the five dams returning to the sea is opened again before autumn, then parts of Jiangdu, Gaoyou, Shiying, and Huai'an counties, as well as all of Xinghua, Taixian, Dongtai, Yancheng, and Funing counties, will become swamps wherever the floods flow, causing hundreds of thousands of acres of crops to be lost and millions of disaster victims to have no way to survive. The impact on the national economy and people's livelihood is so great. For this reason, it is requested that your Excellency telegraph the Canal Engineering Office to ensure that the dams in Gaoyou County that return to the sea are protected as much as possible, even if the water level increases without decreasing, and to extend the time in accordance with the precedents before opening the dams in the 5th and 10th years of the Republic of China, and handle them accordingly. If the weather is clear and the wind is right, and they are fully protected, it will be even more perfect.

Huzhou

The Liu-Sheng Divorce Case Has Been Pronounced: Liu Yanting, a wealthy man from Nanxun Town in Huzhou, was sued last year by his wife, Liu Sheng (daughter of the late Sheng Xingsheng), to the Wuxing Local Branch Court, requesting a divorce from her husband, Liu Yanting, due to certain reasons, and demanding that the defendant, Liu Yanting, pay the plaintiff over 800,000 yuan in alimony. The court investigated and debated the case several times, and finally granted the divorce. The judgment was pronounced yesterday. The main text of the judgment is recorded below: The marriage between Liu Sheng and the defendant, Liu Yanting, is granted a divorce. Liu Yanting shall pay Liu Sheng 52,200 yuan in alimony after the divorce and 10,000 yuan in dowry. The plaintiff's remaining claims are rejected. The litigation costs of the first instance shall be borne by the plaintiff, Liu Sheng, for eight-tenths and by the defendant, Liu Yanting, for two-tenths.

Pishan Flood Disaster Request to Ban Slaughter: In the Pishan Village area outside the North Gate of this city, there are a total of thirteen agricultural dikes. Due to continuous rain, the villagers have been sounding gongs day and night to gather the masses to monitor the dikes. However, the dikes are only a few inches away from the river water. Therefore, more than 100 farmers gathered with Village Chief Shen of the village and came to the Wuxing County Government in the city at around 1:00 PM today, the 29th, to report the flood disaster and request that the County Magistrate issue an order to ban slaughter.

County Party Headquarters Requests Repayment of Education Funds Owed by the Municipal Government

▲ From July of the 17th year to June of the 20th year

▲ A huge debt of 36,000 yuan

Since the separation of Shanghai County from the municipality, all county-level education funds, after consultation between the province and the city, were to be subsidized by the municipal government at 1,000 yuan per month. However, the municipal government violated the agreement and failed to issue the funds, accumulating a debt of 36,000 yuan from July of the 17th year to the end of June of the 20th year. Yesterday, the county executive committee submitted a request to the provincial reorganization committee, asking the provincial government to forward it to the Shanghai municipal government, urging compliance with the agreement and repayment of the owed subsidies. The original request is as follows: The request concerns the Shanghai municipal government violating the municipal agreement by failing to issue subsidies for county-level education funds. It is requested to forward the letter to the provincial government and then to the national government to implement the agreement and allocate the subsidy funds to maintain education. Upon investigation, Article 5, Section E of the resolutions of the conference on the division of administrative power between the province and the city stipulates that the municipal government will subsidize Shanghai County's education funds by 1,000 yuan per month. This agreement was made because the county's annual revenue has decreased since the separation from the municipal government to compensate it, which should be honored by both parties to ensure fairness. However, the municipal government has not complied with the agreement and has failed to issue the subsidies for county-level education funds. It is estimated that the subsidy has been in arrears, calculated from July of the 17th year to the end of June of the 20th year, totaling 36,000 yuan. This not only hinders the development of county education, but also because both the province and the city are under the National Government, the agreement reached should naturally have absolute legal effect. Therefore, the county's third full congress of representatives resolved to recover the educational subsidy owed to it by the Shanghai Municipal Government. We hereby request your commission to forward this to the provincial government, and then to the Shanghai Municipal Government, to implement the provincial-municipal agreement, to clear the previously owed education subsidy, and to provide subsidies on schedule according to the agreement in the future, so as to respect the agreement and maintain education.

Chih-Chih College Approved for Registration

Chih-Chih College has been established for seven years. The board of directors had been registered earlier. In the spring of this year, the school purchased land for construction in the water and electricity district, building a three-story dormitory and auditorium capable of accommodating over a thousand people, a two-story classroom, library, and office building, and three attached bungalows. In addition to all necessary sanitary facilities, it has everything it should have. It also ordered two generators from Germany to supply electricity to the entire school and drilled an artesian well, using a motor to pump water to supply water. In terms of curriculum, the heads of various departments have also jointly revised and reorganized it to strive for perfection. The new school buildings have been completed and were inspected by officials from the Ministry of Education last month, who deemed them satisfactory. It was recently approved by the Ministry of Education. The registration order of the school has been relayed to the school by the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau for notification.

China Association Lost in the Class A Tennis League of the Central Ground Yesterday

▲ Lost to South Grassland Six to Nine

▲ Qiu Jiang's Complete Victory Was to No Avail

—China Association Will Battle West Youth Tomorrow—

The China Tennis Association played a makeup game of the Class A Grass Court Tennis League against South Grassland at the China Tennis Court yesterday afternoon. A large crowd watched. As a result, the China Association lost to South Grassland by a score of six to nine. However, the first group of the China Association, Qiu Feihai and Jiang Daozhang, won against the South Grassland stars Huite group. Huite's poor pairings were ineffective. Qiu Feihai received the most praise, and Jiang's performance was more satisfactory than usual, with powerful shots. Unfortunately, the second and fifth groups were completely defeated, greatly hurting the China Association's morale. In addition to Qiu Jiang's three points, Yu Liu scored one point, and Qian Tu scored two points, totaling six points. South Grassland's victory lies in its average talent. The team had previously won against the French Chamber of Commerce by a score of eight to seven and against North Grassland by a score of eleven to four, which is not a bad record. The China Association is scheduled to play a makeup game against West Youth at the China Tennis Court at 5:00 PM tomorrow.

Sheng Pinchen Announces the Launch of the East China Team, Aiming to Promote Sports and Develop National Glory in Football

—One of the talks at last night's social banquet

▲ Lineup is set—May need to be changed in the future

Since the strength of the Yuehua Football Team declined and its star players scattered, the Shanghai football scene has become depressed. Suddenly, there is good news. Sheng Pinchen, Shen Yiqing, Sheng Ping, Xu Zhendong, Huang Dazhong, Zhou Jiaqi, Dai Linshu, Dai Linzhao, Wei Chengrui, and 24 others have launched the East China Football Club.

Last Night's Social Banquet of the East China Association ○ Committee Chairman Mr. Sheng Pinchen (Photo by this Newspaper)

Almost all football talents with special skills in the East China region have been recruited. Even Chen Guangyao and Cao Guicheng from Hong Kong, and Sun Sijing from Tianjin, have heard the news and come to join. Judging by its strength, at least to the minimum extent, it is sure to surpass Yuehua. At 8:00 PM last night, the association invited members of the sports and journalism communities to hold a social gathering at the New World Restaurant. More than thirty people attended. Halfway through the dinner, Sheng Pinchen, the founder and chairman of the association, stood up and announced the association's founding purpose, which is to "promote sports" and "develop national glory." In other words, they hope to achieve a superior position in the Chinese and Western football community in Shanghai, in order to enhance international reputation. Also, in this era of Yuehua's decline, there is a need for an organized sports institution to step forward and shoulder this important task. The founders earnestly hope for the support of comrades in the sports and journalism communities. Committee member Xu Zhendong said that the association pays close attention to the amateur status of the players, and the association's affairs and finances are all public. In short, the founders and players of the association all embrace a clean and honest spirit, with no meaning of false borrowing or exploitation included in it. This will be proven when the constitution is published in the future. Finally, Sun Daosheng gave a reply on behalf of the guests, saying that the development of various sports in Europe and the United States is half due to the widespread establishment of sports organizations. In recent years, there have also been gentlemen and merchants in our country who are enthusiastic about sports and have resolutely organized themselves, such as Cheng Yize of the Youyou Sports Association, which has achieved success, and Sheng Pinchen of the East China Association, which announced its founding purpose today. They are truly pioneers in the development of Chinese sports. In addition to expressing our sympathy, we should also provide them with considerable assistance in practice, and move towards a bright future together. We not only hope for their development. According to Chen Yutian of the association, the team roster is roughly as follows, but there may be changes in the future. For example, there is talk that Chen Zhenhe may join the aviation industry. Whether he will come or not will be determined at a later date, so it cannot be regarded as the official lineup.

Let's observe the lineup.
