Local News

Yesterday's Takeover of the French Concession Court

▲ The Two Presidents Are Scheduled to Take Office at the Court Today

▲ The French Consul General Expresses Great Satisfaction

The reorganization of the French Concession Court into the Third Branch of the High Court and the Second Branch of the Special District Local Court is scheduled to formally establish today. Yesterday, Liang Renjie, the President of the High Court, and Ying Shi, the President of the Special Court, went to take over the French Concession Court and the prison. All personnel of the two courts will report to the court today. The situation yesterday is recorded below:

▲ Turnover Personnel: The personnel who participated in the takeover and handover yesterday included Yang Zhaoyun, the representative of the Judicial Administration Department, Secretary Xiao Jinfang, the newly appointed President of the Third Branch of the Jiangsu High Court Liang Renjie, Chief Prosecutor Peng Wangye, the President of the Second Branch of the Shanghai Special District Local Court Ying Shi, Chief Prosecutor Chen Beisan, Warden Xie Fuzi, and others from the Chinese side. The French side included French Consul General Gamgerlin, former French Concession Court Assessor Tu Ge, Assessor Jia Dang, French Public Works Bureau Acting Director General Jia Si, former French Concession Court Warden Gu Sai, and other staff members.

▲ Meeting Between the Two Parties: At about 6:00 PM yesterday,

Liang, Ying, Peng, Chen and other officials from the two courts, as well as the President of the Special District Court Yang Zhaoyun and National Government Secretary Xiao Jinfang, led the takeover staff to the French Concession Court. French Consul General Gamgerlin and French Concession Court Assessor Tu Ge came out to meet them. Consul General Gan soon left. Tu Ge led Liang, Ying, and others to various places inside the court to inspect the document delivery room, the Chinese Civil Division, the Chinese Criminal Division, the Chinese and Foreign Civil Division, the Chinese and Foreign Criminal Division, the Civil and Criminal Division without Consular Jurisdiction, the Prosecutor's Office, and other places. Tu Ge also gave detailed instructions and explanations. ▲ Takeover Situation: During the takeover, Xiao Jinfang allocated the personnel taking over the French Concession Court. The takeover was divided into several parts, including the takeover of funds, the takeover of buildings, and the takeover of miscellaneous items. The takeover was carried out by clerks and translators from the Special Court. After all the documents and files of the French Concession Court were transferred to the Chinese court, it became the new court's office. Therefore, all the handover procedures were carried out there. However, because it was already late at 6:00 PM and there were many

Chinese and French Personnel Taking Over the French Concession Court. (Photo by this newspaper)

items, it was not easy to take over everything at once. Therefore, President Liang and others decided to completely transfer all items from the French Concession Court to the new court and check them again this morning. For the night, they sent clerk Pan Shou-hien and translator Yang Lan-chun to take responsibility for safekeeping.

▲ Takeover of the Prison: The prison of the French Concession Court was also taken over by our side. Yesterday morning at 10:00 AM, President Liang and President Ying took a car to inspect the French prison on Route Massenet and Rue Sévère. At 6:00 PM, Warden Xie Fuzi led more than sixty prison guards to take over the prison. President Liang and others also went to discuss the takeover situation with the French Warden Gouget. In the prison, Chinese police were sent to guard all the posts that were originally guarded by French prison guards. The number of police was the same as the original number of French prison guards. After Chinese police had been stationed at all the French posts, the French police withdrew completely. At this point, the takeover of the prison was completed. This was like a shift change.

▲ Remarks by the French Consul: After meeting President Liang and others, French Consul General Gamgerlin made remarks, saying that he was deeply satisfied to transfer the French Concession Court to China according to the wishes of the French side. In the future, if the Chinese side encounters any difficulties with the French Concession Court, he will do his best to help or offer suggestions to the Chinese authorities.

▲ Remarks by Mr. Liang: President Liang also spoke in French to the French Assessor Tu Ge, saying that this takeover was not only fortunate for China, but also fortunate for France. This is enough to enhance the friendship between China and France and connect the feelings between the two countries. The French Concession Court has achieved excellent results so far. We deeply appreciate the spirit of the French side acting as an agent for China, and at the same time, we hope that Mr. Tu Ge will give us some advice. Mr. Tu Ge is willing to serve as an advisor to the new court (there were provisions for the position of advisor in the agreement). This point may become a reality.

▲ Taking Office Today: This morning at 9:00 AM, President Liang, President Ying, and others will go to the new court to take office. Because they rushed to complete the handover procedures last night, the time was too short, and various trivial matters were not cleared up. Therefore, today the two presidents will supervise the staff to handle the unfinished matters after the handover. Most of the cases in the court have been suspended, but important and urgent cases will still be heard as usual.

▲ Atmosphere of the New Location: The offices of the two courts, the High Court is located at Heng'ai Lane on Rue Victor Heushem and the Special Court is located at He Meifang on Rue Sévère (i.e., behind the French Concession Court). Last night, people were already moving all the wooden furniture and equipment into the new locations and hanging up brand-new white-bottomed black-lettered signs. The buildings were also thoroughly renovated, looking brand new and adding a vibrant atmosphere. From now on, the judicial organs of the three worlds in this city will be under the central judicial rule, and the name of the French Concession Court will become a historical past.

▲ French Lawyers: After the reorganization of the French Concession Court, the French Public Works Bureau specially appointed lawyers Fei Xizhen and Gu Shouxi as the legal representatives of the French police. Lawyers Fei and Gu have already accepted formal letters of appointment and will start working immediately.

▲ French Consul Presents Medals: Yesterday afternoon at 5:00 PM, French Consul General Gamgerlin and Deputy Assessor Tu Ge, Jia Dang, Chinese Assessors Zhu Qi, Gong Xiang, Tang Zaili, and the entire Chinese and Western staff of the prosecutor's office gathered at the French Concession Court. First, French Consul General Gamgerlin gave a speech to all the Chinese and Western staff. Then, he awarded the medals issued by the French government to Vidal, the head of the prosecutor's office, and Zhu Taizeng, the former clerk of the prosecutor's office, and Wang Yintao and Lu Hairong, the clerks in charge of distribution, for their diligence and commendable work. Consul General Gan personally pinned the medals on the chests of the four men as a reward.

Temporary Alert Today

▲ Precautions by the Chinese Concession Authorities

Today is the so-called "August 1st" Red Memorial Day. At a time when the suppression of the Communists and the rebellion is urgent, the military and police authorities in the Chinese concession of this city have temporarily announced an alert for the sake of maintaining peace in the rear. Garrison troops in all parts of the North and South City have been increased to send out patrol teams, and armed soldiers have been stationed at all important passes on the border between the Chinese and foreign concessions. The district teams under the Municipal Public Security Bureau have also increased the number of police on duty, paying attention to the passers-by and inspecting them as the situation dictates. Patrol teams have been increased to patrol the streets. The water patrol team of the Huangpu River has also stepped up its defenses. The concessions have also been stricter than usual.

Ma Fuxiang Talks About the Suppression of Shi Yousan

▲ The Isolated Troops of Shi Can Be Expected to Be Annihilated

▲ The Northeastern Air Raids Are Effective and Even Faster

Ma Fuxiang, Chairman of the Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Commission, came to Shanghai the day before yesterday. The reporter from Xin Sheng She visited him at the Cangzhou Hotel yesterday and interviewed him in detail about the central government's suppression of Shi Yousan. A record of the conversation is as follows: ▲ Shi's Rebellion Can Be Easily Resolved Shi's army only has 30,000 to 40,000 men, of which only 20,000 to 30,000 are able to fight against the central and northeastern armies. However, Shi's army only wants to advance aggressively without considering the rear, which will inevitably lead to the isolation of the troops. Therefore, it is very easy to resolve. Moreover, the northeastern army is very strong and uses a large number of aircraft to attack. The destruction of Shi's troops can be expected soon. Now I am receiving a telegram from Cao Zhusan, a member of the Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Commission and Director-General, sent from Peiping and forwarded by Nanjing, reporting that the northeastern army's bombing by aircraft has been very effective. While speaking, he showed the telegram to the reporter. The original text is as follows: "To the Chairman of the Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Commission, Ma. The confidential telegram has been sent. There was only a small contact yesterday in the Qingfengdian area, and there has not yet been a formal battle. The northeastern army is emphasizing air power in this operation. There are already 34 aircraft participating in the front line. They bombed at night using moonlight, which has been very effective. Please quickly send 30 sheets of imprinted paper. Ge bows, Jianyin."

▲ Soviet Russian Assistance Regarding the rumor that Shi Yousan's rebellion was supported by the Third International's Russian funds, this is likely to be true. Otherwise, Shi's troops are trapped by lack of funds and have no way to resist the central government. As for the Shanxi army coming out, the rumor that it is in response to Shi and others is completely inaccurate. The Shanxi army is indeed sincerely participating in the suppression of Shi.

▲Please call for National Unity Against Japan and Aid to Overseas Chinese

▲Resolutions of the City Residents' Assembly the Previous Day

According to the Kuomintang News Agency, various circles of citizens in this city held a City Residents' Assembly for Suppressing Communists, Punishing Rebels, Opposing Japan, and Aiding Overseas Chinese at the Public Sports Ground in the South City the previous day. More than 100,000 citizens present unanimously advocated suppressing the Red bandits, punishing the rebels, permanently opposing Japan, and actively aiding overseas Chinese. On the spot, they also resolved to send a telegram to comfort and encourage Commanders Chiang and Zhang, as well as the soldiers on the front lines, to work hard to kill the enemy. They also decided to send a telegram to the whole country to unite against Japan and aid overseas Chinese, support the government's suppression of bandits and punishment of rebels, and other important proposals. These matters were already reported in yesterday's newspaper. It is now learned that the above two telegrams were sent yesterday in the name of the assembly. The original text is as follows:

▲Telegram to All Circles of the Country: Respected Nanjing Central Party Headquarters, National Government, Party Headquarters of all provinces, Municipal Governments of all provinces and cities, all newspapers, and all mass organizations: Since the Northern Expedition of the National Revolutionary Army, the Three Principles of the People have been implemented, and warlords have been eliminated. In just a few years, a unified situation has been established. Although there have been many dangers and hardships, thanks to the concerted efforts of the government and the people, and the arduous struggle, stubborn enemies have been defeated and the chief culprits have been expelled. Just as military pacification and political tutelage were about to begin, rebellions occurred from time to time, and the Red bandits bred and entrenched themselves in Hunan and Jiangxi, becoming increasingly rampant. People's livelihoods have been deteriorating, and construction has been delayed as a result. Chairman Chiang has been working diligently day and night, supervising the troops in Jiangxi. Good news has been spreading repeatedly, and there is hope for sweeping away the bandits. However, Shi Yousan's rebellious and treacherous nature has led him to collude with Japanese imperialism externally, instigating Koreans to discriminate against Chinese and assisting them in making trouble. Internally, he colludes with the remaining Red bandits and the rebellious elements in Guangdong and Guangxi, vainly attempting to provide support. For the past ten days, they have been disturbing Hebei, destroying the national order and becoming the enemy of the people. If this is not punished, where is justice? If this is not punished, where is the law? All the citizens of Shanghai held a City Residents' Assembly for Suppressing Communists, Punishing Rebels, Opposing Japan, and Aiding Overseas Chinese at the Public Sports Ground in this city. More than 100,000 people enthusiastically participated, a sight never seen before. The assembly unanimously resolved to pass the following resolutions: (1) This assembly will send a telegram to comfort and encourage Commander-in-Chief Chiang, Deputy Commander-in-Chief Zhang, and the soldiers on the front lines, to work hard to kill the enemy and achieve complete success in the revolution. (2) A request will be submitted to the Central Government that if Shi's troops abandon their rebellion and return to obedience, they may be allowed to return, but Shi himself must not be tolerated in any way. He must be clearly punished as an example to the world. The citizens of this city are willing to raise 100,000 yuan to reward the capture of Shi. (3) A telegram will be sent to all organizations across the country to rise up in unison, oppose Japan and aid overseas Chinese, and support the National Government in suppressing bandits and punishing rebels. (4) A telegram will be sent to all military and civilian officials across the country to cooperate in the work of suppressing bandits and punishing rebels, in order to quell internal unrest and resist foreign aggression. The assembly also unanimously passed a declaration, which read: (The original text was published in yesterday's newspaper). Subsequently, all the citizens of the city vowed to abide by the points indicated in the declaration and fight to the end. We sincerely hope that all compatriots across the country will unanimously advocate and uphold justice together. It is fortunate for the country, and fortunate for the nation. Respectfully submitted by the Shanghai City Residents' Assembly for Suppressing Communists, Punishing Rebels, Opposing Japan, and Aiding Overseas Chinese.

▲Telegram to Commanders Chiang and Zhang: The Assembly sends a telegram to Commanders-in-Chief Chiang in Nanchang and Deputy Commander-in-Chief Zhang in Beiping, and to all revolutionary soldiers: Since the National Revolutionary Army began its Northern Expedition, five years have passed. During this period, remnants of warlords and subsequent rebellions, and repeated obstruction by imperialists, have been overcome thanks to the steadfast command of the Commanders-in-Chief and the courageous killing of the enemy by all the revolutionary soldiers. The country has been stabilized, and unification has been completed. Just as political tutelage was about to begin and people's livelihoods were about to be stabilized, the rebellions of warlords gave the Red bandits an opportunity to run rampant. The suffering in Hunan has been severe and continues to be so. The disasters have spread to almost the entire country. The Central Government, deeply concerned about the people's hardships, entrusted you, Commander-in-Chief, with the important task of suppressing the bandits. Commander-in-Chief, aware of the Red bandits as a grave internal threat, you have supervised the troops, and all the soldiers have been inspired to fight bravely. Good news has been spreading, and there is hope for suppressing the bandits in the Soviet areas. However, Shi Yousan has betrayed his faith, disregarded morality, lost his mind, and colluded with the Red bandits, relied on foreign aid, and seized the opportunity to raise troops and rebel. Alas, as Japanese imperialism is instigating Koreans to massacre our overseas Chinese compatriots, and the remnants of the Red bandits are still making their last stand, Shi Yousan is acting recklessly, disturbing the North. How can anyone with a conscience tolerate this? If this is not punished, where is justice? If this is not punished, where is the security of the people? The Central Government has been lenient in the past, tolerating evil-doers, but the people have suffered. We hope that you, Commanders-in-Chief, will respect the will of the people, reorganize the troops, and launch a major attack to eliminate these vile elements. Only then can the rebellious elements in Guangdong and Guangxi lose their support, and the Red bandits in Jiangxi and Fujian be unable to prolong their existence. You, Commanders-in-Chief, and all the revolutionary soldiers, have embraced the teachings of the late Premier Sun Yat-sen and have already become the vanguard of the people. Our people will also follow and strive to support you until the stubborn enemies are swept away and the rebel leaders are captured. We hope that within ten days, a great victory will be achieved. The Shanghai City Residents' Assembly, held today, on the anniversary of the national humiliation, respectfully represents three million citizens in extending our condolences and encouragement to you, Commanders-in-Chief, and all the revolutionary soldiers. We also vow to unite as one and become the rearguard of all the revolutionary soldiers. We especially hope that after suppressing the rebellion and eliminating the bandits, the country will be unified, and all levels will work together to resist foreign powers, avenge the killing of our overseas Chinese compatriots in Korea, and wash away the shame of the treaty signed under duress several decades ago. We look up to the wind and await good news. Respectfully submitted by the Shanghai City Residents' Assembly for Suppressing Communists, Punishing Rebels, Opposing Japan, and Aiding Overseas Chinese.

▲Expected to Arrive on September 1st

▲To Study the Implementation of the Factory Law

The Ministry of Industry and Commerce has decided to implement the Factory Law starting today. However, because there were still problems regarding the implementation of the Factory Law in the concession areas, it consulted with the China Branch of the International Labour Office and requested the International Labour Office in Geneva to send representatives to Shanghai to investigate the situation and study the implementation of the Factory Law. It is now learned that the International Labour Office has dispatched Mr. Pône and Mr. Anthonsen as representatives, who set off from Geneva yesterday with their entourage to come to Shanghai. Preparing for the Establishment of an Urgent Relief Association for Flood Disasters in Various Provinces

Xu Jingren, Chairman of the Relief Committee, stated that this year's continuous rain has caused disasters in sixteen provinces, including Sichuan, Guangdong, Hunan, Hubei, Henan, Anhui, Jiangxi, Fujian, Zhejiang, Jiangsu, Shandong, Hebei, Liaoning, Jilin, Heilongjiang, and Rehe. The disaster area is vast, and the disaster situation is enormous, unprecedented in a century. In addition to requesting the government to quickly raise huge funds for relief, he also appealed to the society. On July 28th, he, along with Wang Ting and Li Zucuo, permanent members of the committee, invited dignitaries from all walks of life to a meeting at Jue Lin to discuss ways to relieve the flood disasters in various provinces. It was decided on the spot to establish the Shanghai Fundraising Association for Urgent Relief of Flood Disasters in Various Provinces and to hold a preparatory meeting at Renji Hall yesterday. More than 20 people attended, including Pan Gongzhan (representing Feng Liutang), Wu Yunzhai, Wang Yiting, Wen Lanting, Wu Zhihao, Zhang Gongquan (representing Jin Bicheng), Li Zushen, Huang Hanzhi, Chen Guangfu (representing Zheng Jianfeng), Shi Liangcai (representing Ma Yinliang), Xu Qianlin, Zhang Xianqing, and Ha Shaofu. Chen Binhe, etc. Wang Yiting chaired the meeting and discussed fundraising methods in great detail. It was also decided to invite Shanghai celebrities from all walks of life, as well as various trade associations, native place associations in Shanghai, and charitable organizations to a dinner at the City Chamber of Commerce at 6:00 PM on August 6th to report on the disaster situation in various provinces and distribute disaster situation tables. At the same time, the Urgent Relief Association for Flood Disasters in Various Provinces will be formally established. It is said that Chairman Xu is going to Beijing to request funds from the Central Government for disaster relief and to request the issuance of 10 million yuan in disaster relief public bonds. He has also telegraphed Chairman Chiang to ask for approval and is expected to rush back to Shanghai on the 3rd to discuss all matters related to the organization of the Flood Disaster Urgent Relief Association with all sectors of society.

Inspection of Yongbo Ships for Epidemics

▲Implementation Begins Today

The Health Bureau and the Shanghai Port Quarantine Office, due to the discovery of true cholera in Ningbo, will send medical officers to inspect ships coming to Shanghai from Ningbo, starting on August 1st, to prevent the spread of the disease. They will also provide free cholera vaccinations to facilitate prevention. They have separately notified various shipping companies. Large shipping companies such as China Merchants, Sanbei, Ningshao, and Taikoo are very clear about the importance of this kind of epidemic prevention measures and are doing their best to support and promote them.

Wu Liande Talks About the Recent Situation of Cholera

▲Two Deaths in the Public Concession

▲Cases Also in Zhoupu, Pudong

According to Dr. Wu Liande, Shanghai and other places have had continuous rain this year, which can easily lead to epidemics. Therefore, since the beginning of summer, the health authorities in Shanghai City, the Public Concession, and the French Concession, in view of the effectiveness of last year's epidemic prevention cooperation, have made even greater efforts in cholera prevention this year. The health authorities in the French Concession began preventive vaccinations on April 1st. Other Chinese areas and the Public Concession also began holding them on May 1st. To date, 500,000 people have been vaccinated. At the same time, more attention has been paid to those suffering from gastrointestinal diseases to see if they have any signs of cholera. There have been two cases of cholera in the Public Concession, both of whom have died. One was discovered on July 24th, and the other was discovered on July 28th. However, it has not yet been confirmed whether the two cases were true cholera. Therefore, Shanghai can still be considered a non-epidemic port. However, in Zhoupu Town, Pudong, which is about 30 li from Shanghai and has a population of about 14,000, two children have been found to have cholera. Both are about five or six years old. Zhao's young son developed cholera symptoms on the 29th of this month and died the next day. The Central Health Laboratory (Director Dr. Chen Muyi) confirmed that the rice-water-like excrement he discharged contained true cholera bacteria. The father of the deceased also died a few days ago with the same symptoms. Another child, surnamed Song, developed cholera symptoms on the 30th of this month and was sent to the hospital. The results of the examination of his excrement also contained true cholera bacteria. Because Zhoupu Town is directly under the jurisdiction of Nanhui County and does not belong to the scope of the Shanghai Municipal Government, Director Hu of the Health Bureau is negotiating with the local authorities to select and send doctors to assist in the prevention and has begun vaccinating all families in Zhoupu. All passengers on the small trains from Pudong to Zhoupu and all people traveling between Shanghai and Pudong must be vaccinated. Due to the surge in river water, ferry services have been temporarily suspended, so the focus of prevention has had to shift to the railway transportation area. There is a hospital in the area with ten beds, but preparations have been made to increase the number of beds at any time when necessary to facilitate the work of doctors and nurses. Shanghai and Zhoupu are very close, which is why the Chinese health authorities urgently want to eliminate the cholera before it spreads. Because cholera has been discovered in Ningbo, officials have gone to Wusong to administer cholera vaccinations to passengers coming to Shanghai from Ningbo. The local health authorities have now adopted the above-mentioned methods of early prevention, so I hope that cholera can be eliminated in the future.

Business Tax on Department Stores Approved for Reduction

▲Result of the Trade Association's Petition

The Shanghai Department Store Trade Association previously stated that the business tax rate was too high to bear and contradicted the Ministry of Finance's interpretation. It sent representatives to Beijing to petition and also sent a letter to the Tax Rules Research Committee of the City Chamber of Commerce, requesting that it forward a letter to the City Authorities to request a reduction. After going, it received a reply from the City Chamber of Commerce saying, "In direct reply, your letter of July 15th was received, stating business difficulties and requesting a special letter to the City Authorities to reduce the tax rate in accordance with the rate for foreign goods businesses. This Association has submitted a special letter to the Shanghai Municipal Finance Bureau's Business Tax Preparation Office, requesting a review and decision. Now, a letter from the Office, Zheng Zi No. 5, states: 'Your Association's letter requesting that the business tax on department stores be changed to the tax rate for Beijing-Guangzhou foreign goods businesses has been submitted for review. The Ministry of Finance has issued an order to investigate and reply to the Bureau, stating that the nature of department stores is the same as that of Beijing-Guangzhou foreign goods businesses and should be allowed to be taxed at a rate of 0.2% of turnover to show fairness.'" Minutes of the Shanghai Municipal Council Meeting

▲Taxation of Unregistered Land

▲Suggestions for Adding a Public Welfare Department

Land originally owned by Chinese people in the concession, not registered in the name of foreign merchants at the consulate, and not rebuilt as Western-style houses, is collectively referred to as unregistered land. The Board of Directors of the Shanghai Municipal Council of the Public Concession raised this issue for discussion at its regular meeting on Wednesday evening and decided to submit it to Superintendent Fei Xindun to prepare a summary and make a decision. The beauty of its cabins and the magnificence of its layout are unprecedented on the Sino-American route. It is also very fast, traveling at 19 to 21 nautical miles per hour. The first ship, the President Hoover, has already been completed. This past Tuesday, it left the New Pie to go to New York, where it will be open for public viewing for three days. The engine will be powered by electricity. When it arrives in Shanghai, the company will send invitations to various sectors to visit the ship. The second ship, the President Coolidge, is scheduled to sail on October 15th. Each of these two ships is equipped with aircraft to deliver mail.

▲Resumption of Service of the Shenhu Small Steamer The Shenhu small steamer has been suspended for a long time due to the flood. In order to maintain inland river transportation, the various steamer companies have resumed the service of the Shenhu small steamer yesterday. It is expected that Suzhou and Hangzhou will also be able to find ways to pass through today and tomorrow.

Robbed of Opium The Zi Lin Bao reported that after the Lianhe ship of the Jardine Matheson Company arrived in Shanghai on Wednesday, the captain reported that at around 9:00 PM on Sunday night, the ship arrived at Zhenjiang and berthed alongside the ship. Just as it was about to unload the cargo, a small boat suddenly sailed up. About 30 people in the boat, holding pistols and rifles and wearing ragged military uniforms, boarded the Lianhe ship and used their guns to threaten Chinese and foreign crew members, ordering them not to speak out and sending people to guard the main roads, prohibiting anyone from going up or down. They then went to the engine room to search in detail and found 25 packages of opium, worth about 50,000 yuan. They then transported the opium to the small boat and forced the captain to write a note proving that they had taken nothing else besides the prohibited opium. After obtaining the note, the small boat then fled into the night. The Lianhe ship usually has British warship protection, but there was none this time. There were also no British warships anchored in Zhenjiang that day. It is likely that the gang knew about this, so they dared to come to the ship to rob the opium. However, they did not commit any crimes against the passengers and miscellaneous goods on the entire ship.

Traffic Situation After the Restoration of the Beijing-Shanghai Railway

According to news from both lines, the railway tracks between Zhenjiang and Nanjing stations on the Beijing-Shanghai line and near the Baogai Mountain Tunnel were washed away by rainwater. The Engineering Department of the line supervised the employees to work day and night to repair them, and traffic was restored on the 26th of last month. However, all the construction was temporary in nature, in order to restore traffic quickly. In recent days, trains passing through the area have not yet lifted the restriction of "proceeding cautiously and slowly", so trains are inevitably slightly delayed due to the reduced speed. Special trains carrying gravel and sleepers are now being dispatched to the area for active work. Once the roadbed and tracks are restored and consolidated, trains can travel smoothly.

Both Lines are Taking Careful Precautions

▲The Director of the General Affairs Office Convened a Training Meeting for the Entire Line's Police and Inspectors

The positions of Chief and Deputy Chief Inspectors of Police on both lines were abolished on the 22nd of this month, and all matters of the Inspection Office have been merged into the command of the General Affairs Office of the line. Deputy Chief Inspector Fan Zhaolan was reassigned as a specialist of the Ministry of Railways and is still working at the Railway Bureau, assisting in the management of the Inspection Office. Now, Hu Tianjun, the Director of the General Affairs Office of the line, took advantage of the beginning of the takeover and the urgent defense situation on both lines, and on the afternoon of July 29th, he led specialist Fan Zhaolan to convene all the inspectors for a training meeting in the newly built house at the Shanghai North Station. He generally said that the inspectors must invigorate their spirits, unite with all departments, and pay close attention to defense. Fan Zhaolan also spoke, encouraging all officers to step up defense, straighten up their uniforms, and pay attention to their spirits. The entire body was invigorated, and it is expected that the defense of the line will be further tightened in the future.

工部局對於工廠法態度

The Shanghai Municipal Council, because the National Government is scheduled to implement the Factory Act on August 1st, held a meeting last Wednesday to discuss the matter. Previously, the Municipal Council had expressed its desire to improve industrial conditions and had attempted to pass an appendix to the law banning child labor in 1925. However, due to the lack of labor regulations outside the concession at that time, labor laws were not promulgated within the concession either. Now that the National Government has announced its labor policy, the Municipal Council can also express its attitude. However, before the Municipal Council decides to adopt and implement the appendix, legal procedures must be completed. As for the need to ban employment, the Municipal Council has never doubted it. At the meeting on July 29th, the Municipal Council unanimously approved the principle of labor regulations. However, because the scope of the Factory Act promulgated by the National Government is extremely broad, it is believed that it will take a considerable period of time for industry to comply with the standards stipulated in the law. Based on the suggestions of Chinese members, the Municipal Council expressed the opinion that the initial work for the implementation of the Factory Act must include the following items: (1) working hours during the day and night, (2) the age at which young workers can enter factories, (3) rest days and holidays, (4) compensation for industrial accidents and industrial diseases, (5) bonuses, (6) maternity benefits, (7) banning apprenticeships, (8) labor-management discussion bodies, (9) factory records.

China Bank Inspection Report

▲ The Forty-First Time

The 41st Inspection Report of the Issuance Reserve Inspection Committee of the Shanghai China Bank states that the members of this committee, together with the entrusted accountants, in accordance with the rules of this committee, inspected the issuance of Shanghai China Bank and the reserve warehouse for the exchange coupons used by the joint banks. The 41st inspection was conducted at the bank on July 26th, 1931, and the Director of the Currency Department of the Ministry of Finance also joined the inspection. The results of the inspection are listed as follows: Total amount of exchange coupon issuance: 13,361,0686 yuan, including: 68,561,931 yuan issued by this bank, 33,766,931 yuan used by joint banks, and 31,281,824 yuan used by various banks and firms. Except for the portion used by various banks and firms, which is inspected separately according to the original method, this inspection of the portion used by this joint bank is as follows: The amount issued by this bank and used by joint banks is 102,328,862 yuan. The amount of exchange coupon reserve of this joint bank is 102,328,862 yuan, including: 62,000,06315.08 yuan in cash reserve, and 40,320,546.92 yuan in guarantee reserve. The above two items, with the cash reserve accounting for 60% and the guarantee reserve accounting for 40%, were all checked as accurate. In accordance with Article 5 of the rules, this is a formal report. July 26, 1931. Local News Two

黄包車夫拾金不昧

Rickshaw Driver's Honesty in Returning Lost Money

▲ Sincerity and honesty can inspire the world

▲ The loser rewarded him with foreign money and then accepted it.

Rickshaw driver Xu Buyun, 39 years old, from Funing, lives at No. 2 Yongqing Lane, Huining Road, South City. Yesterday, at about 5:00 in the morning, Xu was pulling his rickshaw out of the rickshaw depot, continuing his daily hard work. Suddenly, a young customer came up to him and hired a rickshaw to 61 Lafayette Road, French Concession, Yongxing Niu Zuo. After agreeing on the fare, Xu pulled him to his destination. The young man got off the rickshaw in a hurry, paid the fare, and hurried into a small alley. Xu continued to look for a second customer. Before long, an old man hired a rickshaw to Nanyang Bridge. After the old man got off the rickshaw, Xu glanced at a paper package left on the rickshaw seat. Xu asked the old man urgently, but the old man shook his head and replied that he had not lost anything. Xu opened the package and examined it carefully. What appeared before his eyes was a pile of banknotes, silver dollars, and more than one hundred haoyin coins. However, Xu was honest by nature and did not covet unexpected wealth. He thought that he had only worked twice just now. If it was not left by the old man, it must belong to the young man, the first passenger. He immediately pulled the rickshaw to the entrance of the alley where the young man got off on Lafayette Road, and sat waiting for the loser to come and find him. He waited for a long time, but the young man did not come. In order to cherish his time, Xu went straight to the Second District General Office of the Zhaozhou Road Public Security Bureau to report the situation, and temporarily deposited the 47 yuan and five jiao in silver dollars, 119 jiao in small silver coins, and 16 copper coins in the office, waiting for the loser to claim them. However, it was already noon, so Xu returned home for lunch. As soon as he arrived at Yongqing Lane, the young loser was already waiting there. It turned out that when the young man hired the rickshaw, he had seen Xu pulling the rickshaw out, and expected that the rickshaw driver must live nearby, so he came to wait specially. As soon as Xu saw the young man, he told him the truth and went to the Second District General Office together. After Xu proved that there was no mistake, and the young man stated the number of items lost, which completely matched, Wang District Chief asked in detail. The young man supplied his name as Wei Guozhen, from Nanjing, 22 years old, claiming that he had important matters in the morning, which caused him to forget all the money on the rickshaw. He deeply regretted his carelessness. After Wang District Chief finished asking, he said that the rickshaw driver Xu Buyun worked hard, was honest by nature, and was able to see money and not take it, which was really rare. He immediately praised him and offered him the reward of ten yuan as compensation, which Xu declined in every possible way before accepting it. Although the matter is trivial, it is indeed rare in modern society.

Mrs. Zhang Shiming Responds to Zhou Miaoying

▲ Regarding the case to confirm the mother-son relationship

Zhou Miaoying (i.e., Zhang Zhou Shi) sued Zhang Xu Shi, Zhang Zhou Qu, etc., to confirm the mother-son relationship. In the appeal to the High Court, the respondent Zhang Xu Shi, through lawyers Zhu Sifu, Jiang Yiping, Cai Nipei, etc., responded. The response is as follows:

Regarding the case with Zhou Miaoying (i.e., Zhang Zhou Shi) being sued to confirm the mother-son relationship, the reasons for the response are hereby presented. The appellant in this case is making an unreasonable commotion, requesting to confirm the mother-son relationship. After the first instance judgment of your esteemed court rejected this claim, the appellant shows no remorse and continues to present reasons for dissatisfaction in lengthy documents, hoping to confuse the hearing. However, the truth is undeniable and cannot be misrepresented. The original statement fabricated facts. The respondent Qu An, either because of his young age or out of unwillingness to speak, has not provided detailed accounts. However, the respondent personally witnessed the events and cannot deny the truth or make reckless statements. Here, the most obvious facts and the most absurd arguments in the original appeal are briefly pointed out below: (1) The original statement claims that the appellant gave birth to a son, namely the respondent Qu An, etc. It is found that the appellant gave birth to Qu An in the first year of the Republic of China and another son named Qiaoshi the following year. When the appellant left, the second son was only four years old. Later, he died of meningitis at the age of nine, after being raised by the respondent. This is a well-known fact. Why does the appellant only mention one son? Could it be that she knows she abandoned her children and left without guilt, making it difficult to express? (2) The original statement claims that after Zhang Xu Shi came into the family, she became jealous and abusive, etc. The respondent came to the family in the third year of the reign of Emperor Xuantong of the Qing Dynasty. Qu An was born in the first year of the Republic of China. Therefore, the respondent came to the family long before the appellant had children. If abuse and jealousy were true, how could the appellant have safely given birth and had two sons? (3) The original statement also claims that she was not allowed to live in the same house and was forced to live with relatives, etc. The year the appellant entered the family was the same year the respondent came to the family. From then on, they lived harmoniously in one room and had children. Until the winter of the fifth year of the Republic of China, they lived together for six years. Then, the appellant suddenly took advantage of people's lack of preparedness and disappeared without a trace. Afterwards, tailors were sent everywhere to search for her, but without any news. Who forced her? What does "not allowed" mean? What is the surname of the so-called relative? Such reckless and absurd statements are truly shocking. (4) The original statement claims that the respondent designed an encirclement, not allowing communication with the appellant, with the intention of separating the mother and son in the future. Numerous letters were intercepted by the respondent, harming the natural bond of kinship, etc. The respondent, as a secondary wife, should treat all children as her own. Moreover, she has her own children. Why would she need to separate the mother and son? The appellant was once a prostitute and unfamiliar with family etiquette and restraints. Her sudden departure and the child remaining with the family made her realize that it was irreversible and she did not have undue expectations (as seen in the appellant's letters). Therefore, for several years, there was no news. It was not until after the twelfth or thirteenth year of the Republic of China that she reappeared in Shanghai, first called Huarui, then Xiaochen, and finally Huaruiying. The letters mentioned in the original statement were from this period. Someone familiar with her persuaded the late husband, Shiming Gong. However, the late husband believed that she resumed her old profession, showing no respect for his family and sons, and was unwilling to forgive her. This can be seen from the tone of her letters. The original statement's claim of interception is a serious misrepresentation. (5) The original statement also claims that Qu An's engagement to Xu Shi was advocated by the respondent, and when he married, she was not allowed to see the appellant, as if there was no mother-son relationship, etc. Qu An's engagement to Xu Shi was decided by the late husband, Shiming Gong, when Qu An was only six years old. There is a marriage agreement from the astrologer Kang Daji as proof (to be verified during the trial). All matters related to the wedding were presided over by the head of the family. As the head of the family, the respondent naturally took full responsibility. Even if the appellant were still a member of the family, the respondent would still have the right to make these choices. It is a mistake to consider it a trap. The above points are the factual errors in the original statement, which Qu An did not know in his childhood or knew but was unwilling to say. Therefore, the respondent must clarify these points to avoid distorting the truth. The following are the reasons for dissatisfaction raised by the original statement regarding the first instance judgment's perceived violations of moral and legal regulations. The points of erroneous views are refuted one by one below: (6) The original statement claims that the appellant was forced by the first wife to live with relatives, and the words used by the agent lawyer in the agreement cannot represent the facts, etc. This is nothing more than an attempt to change the facts in order to overturn the agreement. After a agent lawyer is legally appointed, the effect of all actions and words made by the agent directly affects the principal. The appellant can read simple novels. At the time of the agreement, she personally reviewed it in detail from beginning to end and signed it. It has already been attached to the file and closed. All the amounts listed in it have been received by the appellant one by one. (7) The original statement's first instance moral concepts and legal views are even more erroneous, citing ancient and modern evidence, listing five items A, B, C, D, and E, explaining that new laws recognize that the relationship between a biological mother and child cannot be extinguished. The articles cited are not consistent with the facts of this case. The main points are divided into two categories, new law and old law, to avoid complexity. (A) Regarding the new law, Article 13 of the Implementation Law of the Family Section of the current Civil Code states, "The rights and obligations between parents and children shall be governed by the provisions of the Family Section of the Civil Code from the date of implementation of the Family Section of the Civil Code." The only articles in Chapter 3 of the same section that can be regarded as provisions concerning the relationship between parents and children are Articles 1059, 1060, and 1084 to 1090. Other provisions, such as those on guardianship, support obligations, and the right to support, and the status of members of the family council, all include the mother-child relationship, but all are based on whether they are members of the same family group (i.e., family). Now, is the confirmation requested by the appellant referring to all the provisions of the Family Section? The appellant's qualification as a member of the family group has been lost, and there is no possibility of such a relationship arising. If the confirmation requested is simply the four words "mother-child relationship," like the relationship between grandparents and grandchildren and siblings, and is a legal term, then there is no such distinguishing provision in the entire Family Law. It is unknown what the subject matter of the judgment and the scope of execution are. Even the precedents of the Supreme Court cited in item A of the original statement all contain the words "mother-child relationship," but this is only a legal term for investigating the origin of the principle and is by no means the judgment of each case. Even if there are only these four words, reading the original judgment at the time reveals that the two parties still had a dispute, which was used as the object of the request to determine the scope of the judgment. This can be asserted. (B) Regarding the old law, the Tang, Ming, and Qing legal codes state that a married or divorced mother still has the articles of filial piety and posthumous gifts with the children of her former husband. The family of etiquette has always advocated caution and is by no means without distinction. The commentary on the chapter on mourning garments in the Book of Etiquette states that the son of a divorced or remarried mother serves her as a wife, and the righteousness says that the divorced mother and the remarried mother are not proper for serving her. The mother of a divorced wife is expected to serve for a year, which means the mother had betrayed the deceased husband, so the period of serving is shortened to one year to honour the deceased husband. In case the husband has passed away, and the divorced mother is also deceased, the son would wear mourning attire, a practice that is not commonly practised, as described in the Book of Great Dai. A divorced mother is most likely sent back to her clan. Cai Shi said that a divorced mother should not be remarried and should observe mourning for her father, which is considered appropriate. If the divorced mother remarries, it means she has severed ties with her former husband and lost her chastity to another person and has also severed ties with her son, and no mourning will be observed. The commentary on the one-year mourning garment states that if the father dies and the stepmother remarries, mourning will still be observed to express the gratitude for the stepmother's upbringing, as stated by Qin Shi Huitian. Cai Shi Dejin said that when the mother remarries, she has severed ties with the father, and the love between mother and son is also severed. Therefore, if the husband dies and the mother remarries, the son will not observe mourning if he does not approve. Jiang Shi Zhaoxi said that the scripture only mentions the remarriage of the stepmother and does not mention the death of the father and the remarriage of the mother. It can be inferred that the remarriage of the stepmother includes the biological mother, and if the son does not approve of the biological mother's remarriage, he will not observe mourning. It can be seen that the appellant in this case separated from the family as a concubine. Her departure was different from a situation where the husband passed away and she could not survive on her own. The circumstances are completely different. She secretly left with her young child. It was not Shiming Gong who sent her away. After she left, the infant was in her arms, and searches were conducted everywhere, but there was no news. Thinking back to her resolute departure, vowing never to return, it is truly shocking. After more than ten years, when she was tired of traveling and wanted to return, she suddenly wanted to count the favors and talk about etiquette. This cannot be allowed. (8) The original statement attacks the errors in the first instance judgment, claiming that the original judgment believed the agreement stated that Qu An could not claim any more benefits, and therefore, based on Article 287 of the Civil Procedure Regulations, it was deemed that a confirmation lawsuit could not be filed, etc. The reason for the original judgment was that the legal relationship was empty and there were no fixed and concrete facts that could be used as the object of the lawsuit. The essential elements of the lawsuit were lacking. Even with the confirmation judgment in Article 287 of the Civil Procedure Regulations, there was no legal benefit. Therefore, this lawsuit could not be filed. The sentences recorded in the agreement, such as "no longer claiming any rights" and "never having any property or other relationship with Qu and his family," were further investigations into the case and were not the cause and effect. As for the obligation of support, which is a provision concerning public interest, even if the person entitled to support has the intention to waive the right, the court cannot consider it valid, etc., this is because the opposing agent lawyer did not hear about it when the agreement was established and only listened to the one-sided claims of his client. At the time of the agreement, the parties had a fact of paying and receiving 40,000 yuan in the name of lifelong support fees. However, the ordinary payment was periodic, while this was a one-time payment. Since it has already been paid once, there should be a record of no property relationship in the agreement to show good faith. The original appeal claimed that this record was a waiver of the right to support, which extinguished the mother-child relationship and was legally invalid. The blood relationship is rooted in nature and cannot be created or extinguished by human power. Therefore, there is a relationship and there is a relationship. The Family Section of the Civil Code regulates the relationship of rights and obligations. Therefore, there is a relationship but no affection. The two are completely different. The original statement confused them, which is wrong. (9) The original statement also claims that this case is the most serious of personal lawsuits, but Qu An did not appear in court, and the original trial did not summon him again. In the appeal trial, he must be ordered to appear in court for questioning, etc. According to the current litigation practice, the lawyer agency system is applied. If the presiding judge considers it necessary for the person to appear in court, he can order the person to appear in court himself. This is not limited to personal lawsuits and depends on the difficulty of resolving the dispute, regardless of the seriousness of the situation. In this case, the appellant's claim of a biological mother-child relationship was not denied by the respondent. The agreement established seventeen years ago can prove this. Therefore, there is no dispute over whether it is a biological relationship. However, whether the plaintiff's request is justified and can be legally established must be investigated. To investigate this issue, there are the case files from the previous case, the records from the first instance of this case, and the pleadings of the agents of both parties, which are clear at a glance. The opposing party insists on requiring the person to appear in court, knowing that the defendant grew up in a traditional family and is unwilling to appear in court because this matter concerns privacy. This is a deliberate attempt to make a meaningless request to coerce him. Playing with the word "serious" already reveals their intentions. (10) The original appeal also states that the respondent is acting as the legal mother, causing Qu An to deny the existence of his biological mother, and there is a need to list her as a defendant, etc. The plaintiff's only request is to confirm the biological mother-child relationship. The son she gave birth to is the main defendant. The claims of deception and encirclement cannot be supported by evidence and are fabricated. Therefore, although the appellant requested that the respondent appear in court, the respondent not only does not need to appear in court but also requests that the point of listing the respondent as a defendant be rejected first. In summary of the above responses, your esteemed court should investigate according to law, uphold the original judgment, reject the appeal, and order the appellant to bear the litigation costs, which is fair and convenient. Respectfully submitted to the Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court. July of the 20th year of the Republic of China. The respondent, Zhang Xu Shi, through agents Zhu Sifu, Jiang Yiping, Cai Nipei.

At Jiangjiatang in the southern part of Hongqiao Town in western Shanghai, a rabid dog suddenly appeared at the beginning of last month, biting anyone it encountered and destroying everything. The Zhabei fire truck rushed to the scene, but fortunately, the house was not damaged, and the truck returned. The residents in the area were frightened. The defendant, Qiu Heqing, has also hired lawyer Gu Jirong to present a defense, requesting cohabitation. Yesterday, Judge Zhao Zhenhai opened a court hearing. Both parties attended court with their lawyers. First, the plaintiff, Qiu Xu Xiuqing, testified that after marrying the defendant, she gave birth to several children, all of whom died young. The defendant has no occupation and wanders around, acting like a hoodlum. I work in a cigarette factory to support myself. The defendant repeatedly forced me to borrow money from people. If I did not comply, I would be abused and beaten. On June 6th, I was attacked with firewood, and my arms and face were injured. The sub-landlords all witnessed it. Because they are afraid of the defendant, they dare not testify to avoid resentment. Therefore, my life is a living hell. All my clothes have been pawned. My monthly wages are also taken away. Such behavior is difficult to endure. I request that the divorce be granted. Next, the defendant, Qiu Heqing, 31 years old, testified that he did not want a divorce. Our relationship has always been good. In July of last year, the plaintiff's father became involved with a woman. Since then, the plaintiff listened to the woman's instigation and opposed me. (Judge asked) What do you do for a living? (Answer) I am a food supplier on a ship. I have not abused her. I can request an investigation. (Judge asked) If you have not abused her, why did the plaintiff file a lawsuit? (Answer) She completely listened to slander. It is not easy for my agent to marry a wife. Even if she is dead, I still want her bones. The judge said, You should go out and persuade your friends to talk to her. Maybe you can reconcile. The plaintiff stubbornly said, I am determined not to. The judge then asked Prosecutor Zhao to attend court to express his opinion. The debate began. The plaintiff's lawyer said that the defendant's nickname is Qiu Liuqiao. From this alone, the defendant's usual behavior can be inferred. The defendant has also repeatedly borrowed money from the plaintiff's father, Xu Senting, and there are IOUs. The defendant's lawyer stood up and argued that the borrowing may have happened, but there was no abuse. He requested that the lawsuit be rejected. The judge believed that the debate was over and awaited the verdict.

Verdict in the Case of the Rickshaw Puller Abducting a Woman

▲ Zhu Debiao Sentenced to One Year in Prison

▲ Sang and Xu Sentenced to Six Months

Zhu Debiao, a rickshaw puller from Jiangbei, conspired with Sang Xiaoliuzi and Xu Erhuzi to abduct Zhuang Zhenying, an 18-year-old woman from Wuxi who had lost her way, at noon on the 23rd of last month. They hid her in the Xi'an Hotel on Xi'an Road and conspired to sell her into prostitution. Sang and Xu attempted to defile Zhenying but failed. The case was discovered and arrested by An Siben and Zhao Lianbi, Chinese detectives from the Hongkou Patrol Room, along with the suspected Cantonese woman Chen Aliu. They were all escorted to the Criminal Court No. 3 of the Special Court for interrogation and trial. Yesterday, Judge Xiao Xiefen presided over the court and sentenced Zhu Debiao to one year in prison, and Sang Xiaoliuzi and Xu Erhuzi to six months in prison each. The number of days of detention before the judgment was determined to be two days for one day of imprisonment. The woman Chen Aliu was found not guilty. Attorney Li Zhishan of the Patrol Room announced that he would abandon the appeal, and she was released in court.
